# cs.SE [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [A Capacity-Aware Parr Model for Agile Projects](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01562v1)
*Pedro E. Colla*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于Parr模型重构的产能感知预测层，用于敏捷项目，通过结合归一化工作量需求和产能轨迹来预测进度、完成时间等，无需假设相同活动路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典工作量分布模型在敏捷环境中因固定或受限产能而无法直接应用，需要一种能考虑产能约束的预测方法。

Method: 将Parr模型重构为产能感知预测层，使用归一化的Parr形状潜在工作量需求与产能轨迹结合，提供离散冲刺公式和校准方法。

Result: 模型能预测总体进度、完成时间、产能缺口和冗余，且参数少，可从Scrum记录校准。

Conclusion: 该模型为敏捷项目提供了一种紧凑、产能感知的预测工具，弥补了经典模型在产能约束下的不足。

中文摘要：经典的软件工作量分布模型，包括PNR族和Parr替代曲线，旨在描述隐含人员配置模式下开发工作量的时间分布。当团队产能固定、部分固定或受外部约束时，它们在敏捷环境中的直接使用受到限制，原始曲线可能规定了组织无法分配的人员需求。本文提出将Parr模型紧凑重构为敏捷项目的产能感知预测层。该贡献有意比完整的项目动力学因果理论更为狭窄。将归一化的Parr形状潜在工作量需求与观察到的或计划的产能轨迹相结合。所得模型预测总体进度、完成时间、产能缺口和产能冗余，而不假设在资源限制下遵循相同的内部活动路径。该模型使用少量参数，如总工作量K、Parr形状参数、可匹配非零初始人员的原点常数c以及产能轨迹。提供了离散冲刺公式，以及从普通Scrum记录中校准的方法，以及针对简单管理基线的滚动原点验证协议。

Original abstract: Classical software effort distribution models, including the PNR family and Parr alter native curve, were designed to describe the time distribution of development effort under an implied staffing pattern. Their direct use in agile environments is limited when team capacity is fixed, partially fixed, or externally constrained, the original curve may prescribe a staff demand that the organization cannot allocate. This paper proposes a compact refactoring of Parr model as a capacity-aware forecasting layer for agile projects. The contribution is deliberately narrower than a full causal theory of project dynamics. A normalized Parr shaped latent effort demand is combined with an observed or planned capacity trajectory. The resulting model forecasts aggregate progress, completion time, capacity deficit, and capacity slack without assuming that the same internal activity path is followed under resource restriction. The model uses a small parameter set such as total effort K, a Parr shape parameter, an origin constant c that can match nonzero initial staffing, and the capacity trajectory. A discrete sprint formulation is provided, together with a calibration method from ordinary Scrum records and a rolling origin validation protocol against simple management baselines.

</details>


### [2] [A Single Patch Is Not Enough: Deterministic Fusion of Repair Candidates](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01597v1)
*Boyang Yang,Xiangliang Hu,Luyao Ren,Yanjun Chen,Bach Le,Tegawendé F. Bissyandé,Haoye Tian*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出PatchFusion，一种确定性原子证据融合方法，通过融合候选补丁的共享编辑原子来选择并构建最终补丁，无需测试结果，显著提升补丁选择性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决pass@k到pass@1的差距，现有方法未能确定性地利用共享编辑原子证据进行选择和构建。

Method: 首先将整个差异的一致性融合到一个修复邻域，选择一个可审计的代表，然后应用证据约束融合（ECF）保留重复的编辑原子并修剪不受支持的部分。

Result: 在SWE-bench Verified上解决426/500个bug，SWE-bench Multilingual上236/300，Defects4J上87/371，优于所有基准方法；恢复41和27个单独源无法解决的bug，ECF增加+5/+6/+9个解决，无回归。

Conclusion: PatchFusion通过跨候选证据恢复更多正确补丁，成本低，接近候选可达上限（96.2%和89.7%）。

中文摘要：现代LLM编码智能体通常用pass@k来评估，但在实际场景中开发者只应用单个最终补丁。这个pass@k到pass@1的差距是一个后生成问题：候选补丁池可能包含正确补丁，但系统必须决定向开发者推荐哪一个。现有的后生成方法主要对完整候选进行排序、用测试过滤或查询LLM裁判，但没有一种方法确定性地重复使用共享的编辑原子证据来同时选择和构建最终补丁。因此，我们提出了PatchFusion，一种确定性的候选补丁原子证据融合方法，在决策时不参考任何测试结果。PatchFusion首先将整个差异的一致性融合到一个修复邻域中，选择一个可审计的代表，然后应用证据约束融合（ECF）来保留重复的编辑原子并修剪不受支持的部分。为了评估这一设置，我们构建了PatchFuseBench，一个固定池基准测试，涵盖SWE-bench Verified、SWE-bench Multilingual和Defects4J的候选补丁。在PatchFuseBench上，PatchFusion在SWE-bench Verified上解决了426/500个bug，在SWE-bench Multilingual上解决了236/300个bug，在Defects4J上达到了87/371个合理补丁，在所有三个基准上优于所有匹配的候选池选择器。PatchFusion恢复了41个和27个单个源无法解决的bug（比最佳单个源多30个和18个）。消融研究表明，ECF通过恢复选择遗漏的池内修复，增加了+5/+6/+9个解决的bug，且观察不到回归，并且PatchFusion的收益在候选池重新采样时保持稳定。在这些互补的多源池上，跨候选证据比我们评估的基于测试和基于LLM的选择器恢复了更多正确的补丁，成本低几个数量级，在两个SWE-bench基准上达到了候选可达上限的96.2%和89.7%。

Original abstract: Modern LLM coding agents are commonly evaluated using pass@k, but developers typically apply a single final patch in real-world settings. This pass@k-to-pass@1 gap is a post-generation problem: a candidate patch pool may contain a correct patch, but the system must decide which one to suggest to developers. Existing post-generation approaches mainly rank whole candidates, filter them with tests, or query an LLM judge, but none deterministically reuse shared edit-atom evidence to both select and construct the final patch. Thus, we propose PatchFusion, a deterministic atomic evidence fusion approach for candidate patches that consults no test outcome at decision time. PatchFusion first fuses whole-diff agreement into a repair neighborhood, selects an auditable representative, and then applies evidence-constrained fusion (ECF) to retain repeated edit atoms and prune unsupported parts. To evaluate this setting, we build PatchFuseBench, a fixed-pool benchmark covering SWE-bench Verified, SWE-bench Multilingual, and Defects4J candidate patches.
  On PatchFuseBench, PatchFusion solves 426/500 bugs on SWE-bench Verified and 236/300 on SWE-bench Multilingual, and reaches 87/371 plausible patches on Defects4J, outperforming every matched candidate-pool selector on all three. PatchFusion recovers 41 and 27 bugs that no single source solves (30 and 18 more over the best single source). Ablation studies show that ECF adds +5/+6/+9 solved bugs by recovering in-pool repairs that selection misses, with no observed regression, and that PatchFusion's gains remain stable as candidate pools are resampled. On these complementary multi-source pools, cross-candidate evidence recovers more correct patches than the test-based and LLM-based selectors we evaluate, at orders-of-magnitude lower cost, reaching within 96.2% and 89.7% of the candidate-reachable ceiling on the two SWE-bench benchmarks.

</details>


### [3] [AgentFlow: Building Agent Dependency Graphs for Static Analysis of Agent Programs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01640v1)
*Shenao Wang,Xinyi Hou,Yanjie Zhao,Xiao Cheng,Haoyu Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: AgentFlow是首个从智能体程序中恢复和分析智能体依赖关系的静态分析框架，通过构建框架无关的智能体依赖图(ADG)支持智能体物料清单生成和提示-工具风险检测等治理与安全分析，在5,399个真实程序中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有静态分析或依赖跟踪工具难以恢复智能体程序中由框架诱导语义（如智能体构造函数、工具装饰器和智能体交接声明）表达的新型依赖关系，因此需要新的静态分析方法。

Method: 提出AgentFlow框架，通过构建Agent Dependency Graph (ADG)将智能体、提示、模型、能力、内存状态和控制策略表示为类型化节点，并捕获组件依赖、控制流和数据流依赖作为类型化边。

Result: 在五个代表性智能体框架和包含5,399个真实世界智能体程序的语料库上，AgentFlow相比现有基于AST的智能体静态分析工具恢复了更丰富的智能体实体和依赖关系，生成了更具依赖感知能力的智能体BOM，并发现了238个污点风格的提示到工具风险。

Conclusion: ADG为理解、治理和保障新兴智能体软件提供了实用基础。

中文摘要：LLM智能体越来越多地作为构建在智能体框架上的源代码应用程序进行开发。这些智能体程序将传统的主机语言代码与框架定义的语义（用于模型、提示、工具、内存和多智能体编排逻辑）相结合。因此，它们的行为不仅依赖于传统的控制流和数据流，还依赖于一类新的智能体依赖关系。这些依赖关系通常以框架诱导的语义形式表达，例如智能体构造函数、工具装饰器和智能体交接声明，这使得现有静态分析或依赖跟踪工具难以恢复它们。在本文中，我们提出了AgentFlow，这是第一个用于从智能体程序中恢复和分析智能体依赖关系的静态分析框架。AgentFlow构建了一个智能体依赖图（ADG），这是一种框架无关的图表示，将智能体、提示、模型、能力、内存状态和控制策略表示为类型化节点，并将其组件依赖、控制流和数据流依赖捕获为类型化边。基于ADG，AgentFlow支持一系列用于智能体治理和安全性的分析，包括智能体物料清单（BOM）生成和提示到工具风险检测。我们为五个代表性智能体框架实现了AgentFlow，并在AgentZoo（包含5,399个真实世界智能体程序的语料库）上进行了评估。我们的评估表明，与现有的基于AST的智能体静态分析工具相比，AgentFlow恢复了更丰富的智能体实体和依赖关系，生成了更具依赖感知能力的智能体BOM，并在真实世界智能体程序中发现了238个污点风格的提示到工具风险。这些结果表明，ADG为理解、治理和保护新兴智能体软件提供了实用基础。

Original abstract: LLM agents are increasingly developed as source-code applications built on agent frameworks. These agent programs combine conventional host-language code with framework-defined semantics for models, prompts, tools, memory, and multi-agent orchestration logic. As a result, their behavior depends not only on traditional control and data flows, but also on a new class of agent dependencies. Such dependencies are often expressed as framework-induced semantics, such as agent constructors, tool decorators, and agent handoff declarations, making them difficult to recover with existing static analysis or dependency tracking tools. In this paper, we present AgentFlow, the first static analysis framework for recovering and analyzing agent dependencies from agent programs. AgentFlow constructs an Agent Dependency Graph (ADG), a framework-agnostic graph representation that represents agents, prompts, models, capabilities, memory states, and control policies as typed nodes, and captures their component-dependency, control-flow, and data-flow dependencies as typed edges. Built on ADGs, AgentFlow supports a range of analyses for agent governance and security, including Agent Bill of Materials (BOM) generation and prompt-to-tool risk detection. We implement AgentFlow for five representative agent frameworks and evaluate it on AgentZoo, a corpus of 5,399 real-world agent programs. Our evaluation shows that AgentFlow recovers richer agent entities and dependencies than existing AST-based agent static analysis tools, generates more dependency-aware Agent BOMs, and uncovers 238 taint-style prompt-to-tool risks in real-world agent programs. These results show that ADG provides a practical foundation for understanding, governing, and securing emerging agent software.

</details>


### [4] [When Agents Do Not Stop: Uncovering Infinite Agentic Loops in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01641v1)
*Xinyi Hou,Shenao Wang,Yanjie Zhao,Haoyu Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出无限智能体循环（IAL）问题，并开发了静态分析工具IAL-Scan来检测LLM智能体项目中的此类故障，在数千个仓库中实现了高精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体在迭代执行中可能因反馈路径未受约束而陷入无限循环，导致成本耗尽、服务拒绝等严重后果，缺乏有效的检测方法。

Method: 提出IAL-Scan，通过抽象智能体代码为与框架无关的Agent IR，构建ALD图恢复反馈路径，并检查路径是否可无限重复到达昂贵或状态增长操作。

Result: 在6,549个仓库中报告74个潜在发现，人工确认68个IAL故障（47个项目），精确率91.9%。

Conclusion: IAL-Scan能有效检测LLM智能体项目中的无限循环故障，具有高精确率，可帮助开发者避免代价高昂的运行失败。

中文摘要：LLM智能体越来越多地依赖迭代执行来通过规划、工具使用、状态更新和智能体协作来完成任务。虽然这种设计实现了灵活的自动化，但它也带来了一类新的故障：当反馈路径没有得到有效约束时，智能体可能会重复执行模型调用、工具、工作流转换或智能体切换。我们将此问题称为无限智能体循环（IALs）。IALs不是普通的编程循环；它们源于智能体逻辑、框架语义、运行时观察和终止机制之间的交互。这种故障可以将单个请求放大为长时间运行的模型和工具执行，导致成本耗尽、模型拒绝服务、上下文增长和重复的外部副作用。我们提出了IAL-Scan，一种用于检测真实LLM智能体项目中IAL故障的静态分析工具。IAL-Scan将异构智能体代码抽象为与框架无关的智能体中间表示（Agent IR），构建智能体循环依赖图（ALDG）以恢复显式及框架诱导的反馈路径，并检查这些路径是否可以无有效约束地重复到达昂贵或状态增长的操作。我们在6,549个LLM智能体仓库上评估了IAL-Scan。它报告了74个潜在发现，其中人工审查确认了47个项目中的68个IAL故障，达到了91.9%的精确率。

Original abstract: LLM agents increasingly rely on iterative execution to solve tasks through planning, tool use, state updates, and agent collaboration. While this design enables flexible automation, it also creates a new class of failures: an agent may repeatedly execute model calls, tools, workflow transitions, or agent handoffs when the feedback path is not effectively bounded. We call this problem Infinite Agentic Loops (IALs). IALs are not ordinary programming loops; they arise from the interaction between agent logic, framework semantics, runtime observations, and termination mechanisms. Such failures can amplify a single request into long running model and tool execution, causing cost exhaustion, model denial of service, context growth, and repeated external side effects. We propose IAL-Scan, a static analysis tool for detecting IAL failures in real-world LLM agent projects. IAL-Scan abstracts heterogeneous agent code into a framework independent Agent IR, builds an Agentic Loop Dependence Graph (ALDG) to recover explicit and framework induced feedback paths, and checks whether these paths can repeatedly reach costly or state growing operations without an effective bound. We evaluate IAL-Scan on 6,549 LLM agent repositories. It reports 74 potential findings, among which manual review confirms 68 IAL failures across 47 projects, achieving 91.9% precision.

</details>


### [5] [Refploit: Facilitating Exploit Construction via Code-Agent Trajectory Repair](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01760v1)
*Zirui Chen,Zhipeng Xue,Jiayuan Zhou,Xing Hu,Xin Xia,Xiaohu Yang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出Refploit框架，通过分析失败代码代理轨迹并指导针对性恢复，显著提升Java漏洞利用复现成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动漏洞复现方法生成的利用常看似成功却未触发真实漏洞逻辑（如替换API），导致虚假成功，需要更可靠的复现机制。

Method: Refploit首先通过差异执行验证代理生成的利用；若无效，则分析复现进度，定位轨迹中已完成子任务和误导方向，推导约束以指导LLM有针对性地恢复轨迹。

Result: 在三个数据集上（143个漏洞，172个参考）以DeepSeek-V4-Flash实现80.2%复现率，相对初始轨迹提升64.3%，优于PoCGen和基于GPT-5.4的Codex等基线。

Conclusion: Refploit能有效从失败轨迹中学习并生成真实可用漏洞利用，且适配其他代码代理仍保持一致提升，证明了其通用性和有效性。

中文摘要：漏洞利用在评估Java库漏洞的下游影响中起着关键作用。虽然一些漏洞附带了公开的利用参考，但由于这些参考通常不完整、非结构化或仅描述部分复现步骤，自动将此类参考转化为可运行的利用仍然具有挑战性。最近的代码代理提供了一种自动化该过程的有前景的方法，但我们的研究表明，它们生成的利用常常看似成功，却未触发实际的漏洞逻辑，例如用自行实现的函数替换易受攻击的API。为解决此问题，我们提出Refploit，一种基于LLM的轨迹恢复框架，用于促进从公开利用参考中复现漏洞。关键见解是，失败的代理轨迹并非完全无用。它可能已经完成了一些复现子任务，同时也揭示了应避免的误导性方向。Refploit首先通过差异执行验证代理生成的利用。当利用无效时，Refploit分析其复现进度，定位与复现进度相关的轨迹片段，并推导约束以指导重点恢复。我们在三个开源Java漏洞数据集上评估Refploit，涵盖143个漏洞的172个利用参考。在DeepSeek-V4-Flash下，Refploit成功复现了138个利用，复现率达到80.2%。与初始生成的轨迹相比，它实现了64.3%的相对改进，并优于最先进的利用生成方法PoCGen以及诸如基于GPT-5.4的Codex等高级代码代理。我们进一步将Refploit适配到另一个代码代理并观察到一致的改进，证明了其通用性。

Original abstract: Vulnerability exploits play a crucial role in assessing the downstream impact of Java library vulnerabilities. While some vulnerabilities are accompanied by disclosed exploit references, automatically reproducing such references into runnable exploits remains challenging because they are often incomplete, unstructured, or only describe partial reproduction steps. Recent code agents provide a promising way to automate this process, but our study shows that their generated exploits often appear successful without triggering the actual vulnerable logic, such as replacing vulnerable APIs with self-implemented functions. To address this, we propose Refploit, an LLM-based trajectory recovery framework for facilitating vulnerability reproduction from public exploit references. The key insight is that a failed agent trajectory is not entirely useless. It may have already completed some reproduction subtasks while also revealing misleading directions that should be avoided. Refploit first validates an agent-generated exploit through differential execution. When the exploit is ineffective, Refploit analyzes its reproduction progress, locates the trajectory segments associated with the reproduction progress, and derives constraints to guide focused recovery. We evaluate Refploit on three open-source Java vulnerability datasets, covering 172 exploit references for 143 vulnerabilities. Under DeepSeek-V4-Flash, Refploit successfully reproduces 138 exploits, achieving a reproduction rate of 80.2%. It achieves a 64.3% relative improvement over the initially generated trajectories and outperforms both the SOTA exploit-generation method PoCGen and advanced code agents such as Codex with GPT-5.4. We further adapt Refploit to another code agent and observe consistent improvements, demonstrating its generality.

</details>


### [6] [KRCA: An Efficient Root Cause Analysis System in Hyper-Scale Microservice Systems via Agentic AI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01788v1)
*Jiamin Jiang,Jingfei Feng,Yu Luo,Qingliang Zhang,Yongqian Su,Wenwei Gu,Shenglin Zhang,Tianyu Cui,Yao Wu,Jielong Huang,Nan Qi,Dan Pei*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出KRCA，一种用于超大规模微服务系统的端到端根因分析系统，通过多阶段流水线（API下钻、骨架因果图、记忆增强多智能体）实现高精度和高效率，在快手生产环境部署后平均诊断时间降低77.3%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RCA方法难以适应超大规模微服务系统的极端动态性和巨大规模，需要一种能平衡诊断准确性与实时效率的端到端系统。

Method: KRCA采用多阶段流水线：首先API级下钻隔离可疑服务，然后从异常指标构建骨架因果图作为结构先验，最后使用记忆增强的多智能体框架验证因果关系并生成故障报告。

Result: KRCA在根因服务定位和故障类型分类上的AC@1分别达0.88和0.79，比最强基线绝对提升至少31%；在快手生产环境部署后平均诊断时间降低77.3%。

Conclusion: KRCA通过结合结构化因果约束与多智能体推理，有效解决了超大规模微服务系统的根因分析挑战，在实际部署中显著提升了诊断效率。

中文摘要：超大规模微服务系统已成为大型互联网公司的标准基础设施。这些系统由大量松散耦合的微服务组成，这些微服务通过持续开发和部署独立演进。这种复杂性使得故障不可避免，需要高效的根因分析（RCA）来帮助站点可靠性工程师（SRE）快速定位根因服务并分类故障类型。然而，现有的RCA方法往往难以适应这些系统的极端动态性和大规模。在本文中，我们提出了KRCA，一个为超大规模微服务系统设计的端到端RCA系统。为了管理巨大的搜索空间，KRCA采用了一个多阶段流水线，首先通过API级下钻来隔离可疑服务。然后，它从异常指标中实例化一个基于骨架的因果图，作为高召回的结构先验，再使用一个记忆增强的多智能体框架来验证因果关系并生成最终的故障报告。通过结合结构化因果约束与多智能体推理，KRCA平衡了诊断准确性与实时生产使用的效率要求。实验结果表明，KRCA在根因服务定位和故障类型分类上的AC@1得分分别为0.88和0.79，比最强基线绝对提升了至少31%。KRCA已在快手生产环境部署超过6个月，平均诊断时间降低了77.3%。

Original abstract: Hyper-scale microservice systems have become the standard infrastructure for large-scale Internet companies. These systems consist of numerous loosely coupled microservices that evolve independently through continuous development and deployment. Such complexity makes failures unavoidable, necessitating efficient Root Cause Analysis (RCA) to help Site Reliability Engineers (SREs) quickly localize root cause services and classify failure types. However, existing RCA methods often struggle to adapt to the extreme dynamism and massive scale of these systems. In this paper, we present KRCA, an end-to-end RCA system designed for hyper-scale microservice systems. To manage the vast search space, KRCA employs a multi-stage pipeline that begins with an API-level drilldown to isolate suspicious services. It then instantiates a skeleton-based causal graph from anomalous metrics to serve as a high-recall structural prior, before utilizing a memory-augmented multi-agent framework to verify causality and generate the final failure report. By combining structured causal constraints with multi-agent reasoning, KRCA employs balances diagnostic accuracy with the efficiency requirements of real-time production use. Experimental results show that KRCA achieves AC@1 scores of 0.88 and 0.79 for root cause service localization and failure type classification, outperforming the strongest baseline by at lease 31% in absolute gains. KRCA has been deployed in Kuaishou's production environment for over six months, reducing the average diagnosis time by 77.3%.

### [7] [Archer: Towards Agentic Review for Compiler Optimizations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01808v1)
*Yunbo Ni,Shaohua Li*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出Archer，首个针对编译器优化的自动化代码审查工具，在LLVM的PR评估中发现大量隐蔽语义错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 编译器频繁更新而专家审查能力有限，导致延迟和隐蔽错误引入，自动化审查面临编译器复杂性的挑战。

Method: 基于代理的代码审查工具Archer，通过义务引导分析和确定性验证守卫确保证据可执行。

Result: 在LLVM的70个开放PR和328个关闭PR中，分别发现21%和11%存在语义错误（如误编译）。

Conclusion: 结果表明大型编译器项目存在严重审查缺口，Archer作为附加审查者具有实际价值。

中文摘要：现代编译器频繁更新，但专家审查能力极为有限，导致集成延迟，甚至在某些情况下，微妙的语义错误进入编译器代码库。使用现代通用代码审查代理自动化代码审查过程可能是可行的，但由于编译器的复杂性，它面临关键挑战。在本文中，我们以LLVM为目标编译器，提出了Archer，这是首个针对编译器优化的自动化代理代码审查工具。Archer通过使用义务来指导分析，并从两端约束代理审查过程，以及一个确定性验证守卫来仅接受有可执行证据支持的发现。我们在最近两个月的LLVM上对70个开放的PR和328个已关闭的PR评估了Archer。审查结果令人震惊且值得关注：Archer发现21%的开放PR和11%的已关闭PR存在错误，即在LLVM中引入了如误编译等语义错误。我们的发现揭示了大型编译器项目中关键审查能力的严重缺口，并展示了Archer作为附加审查者的实际价值。

Original abstract: Modern compilers are frequently updated, but expert review capacity is highly limited, leading to delayed integration and, in some cases, subtle semantic bugs entering the compiler codebase. Automating the code review process with modern general code review agents may be feasible, but it faces critical challenges due to compiler complexity. In this paper, we use LLVM as our target compiler and present Archer, the first automated agentic code review tool for compiler optimizations. Archer constrains the agentic review process from both ends by using obligations to guide analysis and a deterministic validation guard to admit only findings backed by executable evidence.
  We evaluated Archer on 70 open PRs and 328 closed PRs in LLVM from the last two months. The review results are shocking and concerning: Archer discovers that 21% of open PRs and 11% of closed PRs are buggy, i.e, introducing semantic bugs such as miscompilations in LLVM. Our findings expose a critical gap in the capacity for critical review in large compiler projects and demonstrate the practical value of Archer as an additional reviewer.

### [8] [Decoupling Code Complexity from Newcomer Participation: A Causal Study of AI Coding Agent Adoption in OSS](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01810v1)
*Weiwei Xu,Xuanning Cui,Hengzhi Ye,Minghui Zhou*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过双重差分法发现，采用AI编码代理的成熟开源项目并未导致新人流入减少，尽管代码复杂度略有增加。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 担忧AI编码代理会通过吸收简单任务和降低代码可读性而挤出开源项目的新人贡献者。

Method: 利用GitHub代码搜索识别首次提交配置文件的采用AI代理的项目（共1888个），采用双重差分法比较603个有真实采用前期的采用者与匹配的非采用控制组。

Result: 新人流入没有显著下降，入职和留存不变，good-first-issue标签未下降；代码复杂度在Python认知度量上增加约11%，所有语言圈复杂度增加3-4%，但在复杂度上升子集中新人参与未下降。

Conclusion: 在成熟开源项目中，采用AI编码代理不会挤出人类新人，但会使代码略显复杂，所担忧的权衡未出现。

中文摘要：开源项目依赖稳定的新人流入。一个日益增长的担忧是，AI编码代理（如Cursor和Claude Code等通过自然语言指令编写代码的工具）会通过吸收初学者起步所需的简单任务以及使代码更难阅读而将他们挤出。我们为这一担忧给出了因果答案。利用GitHub代码搜索，我们识别出1888个采用了代理的项目（以首次提交配置文件为信号）。我们应用双重差分法，与匹配的非采用控制组进行比较，并将主要分析限制在603个具有真实采用前期的采用者中。我们没有发现挤出证据：在各种估计量下，新人流入在采用后并未出现显著下降（点估计范围从小幅增加到高度保守趋势设定下的轻微且不显著下降），入职和留存率不变，一个稀疏的、相关性的初学者任务指标（good-first-issue标签，我们无法检验其平行趋势）也未下降。所担忧的机制确实存在但脱钩了：采用提高了每个函数的代码复杂度（在Python的认知度量上约为+11%，是先前估计的四分之一；在所有语言的圈复杂度上为+3%至4%），但在复杂度上升的固定单元子集中（Python的认知度量以及所有语言的圈复杂度），新人参与并未下降。这些结果表明，在成熟的开源项目中，采用AI编码代理使代码略显复杂，但并未挤出项目所依赖的人类新人：AI辅助与人类参与之间所担忧的权衡并未出现。

Original abstract: Open-source projects depend on a steady inflow of newcomers. A growing concern is that AI coding agents (tools such as Cursor and Claude Code that write code from natural-language instructions) will crowd them out, by absorbing the simple tasks that beginners start with and by making code harder to read. We give this concern a causal answer. Using GitHub code search we identify 1,888 projects that adopted an agent, signaled by their first commit of a configuration file. We apply difference-in-differences against matched non-adopting controls, restricting the main analysis to the 603 adopters with a genuine pre-adoption period. We find no evidence of crowding-out: across estimators newcomer inflow shows no significant decline after adoption (point estimates run from a small increase to, under the most conservative trend specification, a slight and insignificant dip), onboarding and retention are unchanged, and a sparse, correlational beginner-task measure (good-first-issue labels, which we cannot test for parallel trends) shows no decline. The feared mechanism is real but decoupled: adoption raises per-function code complexity (about +11% on a cognitive metric for Python, a quarter of the prior estimate, and +3 to 4% in cyclomatic terms across all languages), yet in fixed-unit subsets where complexity rose (Python on the cognitive metric, and all languages on the cyclomatic metric), newcomer participation does not decline. These results suggest that, in established open-source projects, adopting an AI coding agent makes code modestly more complex but does not crowd out the human newcomers that a project depends on: the feared trade-off between AI assistance and human participation does not materialize.

### [9] [Understanding Software Defect Prediction: A Large-scale Empirical Study Across Uncertainty Quantification and Performance Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01842v1)
*Ranjun Peng,Xuan Xie,Rubing Huang,Wenbin He,Zhijie Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 大规模实证研究发现，软件缺陷预测中的不确定性量化指标高度依赖于上下文，在跨项目时相关性减弱或反转，因此需针对特定性能目标评估UQ并独立评估校准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 常见的不确定性量化（UQ）指标是否可靠地指示软件缺陷预测分类器的性能与校准尚不清楚。

Method: 评估了5个UQ指标、6个性能指标和3个校准指标，使用16个分类器，在36个数据集上进行项目内缺陷预测（WPDP）和32个数据集上进行跨项目缺陷预测（CPDP）的实证分析。

Result: UQ高度依赖上下文；WPDP下UQ与假阳性率和AUC相关性更一致，但与MCC、F1等指标相关性较弱；性能和校准相关但不可互换；CPDP下许多UQ-性能与UQ-校准相关性减弱或反转，不确定性信号不能可靠跨项目转移。

Conclusion: UQ应针对特定性能目标评估，校准需独立使用多个指标，跨项目转移的概率应在指导质量保证决策前重新验证。

中文摘要：软件缺陷预测（SDP）分类器产生用于检视优先级排序、阈值调整和风险沟通的概率。基于概率的不确定性量化（UQ）表征预测置信度，但常见的UQ指标是否可靠地指示性能和校准尚不清楚。我们对SDP中基于概率的UQ进行了大规模实证研究。我们评估了五个UQ指标、六个性能指标和三个校准指标，涉及16个代表性分类器。我们在两种预测设置下分析了这些关系：使用36个基准数据集的项目内缺陷预测（WPDP）和使用32个特征兼容数据集的项目间缺陷预测（CPDP）。结果表明，UQ高度依赖于上下文。在WPDP下，UQ与假阳性率和AUC的相关性比与MCC、F1分数和其他指标的相关性更一致；这些相关性也随分类器类别和数据集集合的变化而变化。性能和校准相关但不可互换；具有强区分能力的分类器仍可能表现出较大的校准误差。在CPDP下，一些UQ-性能和UQ-校准相关性减弱或反转，表明不确定性信号不能可靠地在项目间转移。因此，UQ应针对特定的性能目标进行评估。校准应使用多个指标独立评估。在指导质量保证决策之前，应对转移的概率进行重新验证。

Original abstract: Software defect prediction (SDP) classifiers produce probabilities used for inspection prioritization, threshold tuning, and risk communication. Probability-based uncertainty quantification (UQ) characterizes prediction confidence, but whether common UQ metrics reliably indicate performance and calibration remains unclear. We conducted a large-scale empirical study of probability-based UQ for SDP. We evaluated five UQ metrics, six performance metrics, and three calibration metrics for 16 representative classifiers. We analyzed these relationships under two prediction settings: within-project defect prediction (WPDP), using 36 benchmark datasets, and cross-project defect prediction (CPDP), using 32 feature-compatible datasets. Results showed that UQ was highly context-dependent. Under WPDP, UQ correlated more consistently with false positive rate and AUC than with MCC, F1 score, and other metrics; these correlations also varied across classifier categories and dataset collections. Performance and calibration were related but not interchangeable; classifiers with strong discrimination could still exhibit large calibration error. Under CPDP, several UQ-performance and UQ-calibration correlations weakened or reversed, indicating that uncertainty signals do not reliably transfer across projects. Thus, UQ should be evaluated against specific performance objectives. Calibration should be assessed independently using multiple metrics. Transferred probabilities should be revalidated before guiding quality-assurance decisions.

### [10] [Technical Debt Friction for Maintenance Prioritization: An Industrial Multi-Case Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01850v1)
*Simeon Tverdal,Phu Nguyen,Arda Goknil,Antonio Martini,Markus Borg,Adam Tornhill*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过多案例工业研究提出了技术债务摩擦作为优先级排序概念，发现它能帮助从业者识别维护负担区域，但需结合上下文和互补视图使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有软件分析（如代码健康度、热点区域）未能充分捕捉实际变更体验负担，需要更好的概念来识别维护和重构的优先区域。

Method: 在多个工业案例中与从业者进行结构化走查会议，使用代码健康度、热点区域、耦合性、重构目标和社会技术视图等分析工件。

Result: 技术债务摩擦与已知问题区域和后续维护关注的文件一致，但实际相关性依赖上下文；项目层面分析显示摩擦分布可能揭示更广泛的维护模式。

Conclusion: 技术债务摩擦是有前景的决策支持概念，但需结合上下文知识和支持证据才能最有效。

中文摘要：软件密集型组织需要有效的方法来识别维护和重构工作将在何处产生最大的实际效益。尽管代码健康度、热点区域和耦合性等软件分析提供了有价值的信号，但它们并不总能捕捉到实际中减缓软件演化的变更体验负担。本文提出了一项关于技术债务摩擦的多案例工业研究，将其作为优先级排序概念，用于识别技术债务最强烈影响维护和演化的地方。我们调查了从业者如何解释这一概念，摩擦相关分析是否与感知的维护痛点和重构需求一致，以及摩擦在个体重构候选之外能提供哪些更广泛的维护和演化见解。为此，我们与多个工业案例中的从业者进行了结构化走查会议，使用了包括代码健康度、热点区域、耦合性、重构目标和社会技术视图在内的分析工件。我们的发现表明，从业者普遍认为技术债务摩擦对于推理维护负担是有用的，尤其是当与互补的技术和社会技术视图一起解读时。在文件层面，摩擦通常与已知的问题区域一致，并且在多个案例中与后来得到维护关注的文件一致，尽管其实际相关性强烈依赖于上下文。此外，我们的探索性项目层面分析表明，摩擦分布可能揭示更广泛的维护和演化模式。这些结果表明，技术债务摩擦作为决策支持概念是有前景的，但在与上下文知识和支持证据一起使用时最为有效。

Original abstract: Software-intensive organizations need effective ways to identify where maintenance and refactoring efforts will yield the greatest practical benefit. Although software analytics such as code health, hotspots, and coupling provide valuable signals, they do not always capture the experienced burden of change that slows software evolution in practice. This paper presents a multi-case industrial study of technical debt friction as a prioritization-oriented concept for identifying where technical debt most strongly affects maintenance and evolution. We investigate how practitioners interpret the concept, whether friction-related analysis aligns with perceived maintenance pain points and refactoring needs, and what broader maintenance and evolution insights friction can provide beyond individual refactoring candidates. To this end, we conducted structured walkthrough sessions with practitioners across multiple industrial cases using analysis artifacts including code health, hotspots, coupling, refactoring targets, and socio-technical views. Our findings show that practitioners generally considered technical debt friction useful for reasoning about maintenance burden, especially when interpreted together with complementary technical and socio-technical views. At the file level, friction often aligned with known problematic areas and, in several cases, with files that later received maintenance attention, although its practical relevance depended strongly on context. In addition, our exploratory project-level analysis suggests that friction distributions may reveal broader maintenance and evolution patterns. These results indicate that technical debt friction is promising as a decision-support concept, but most effective when used with contextual knowledge and supporting evidence.

### [11] [Regression Accumulation in Multi-Turn LLM Programming Conversations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01855v1)
*Yonghui,Huang,Lin Ma,Amjed Tahir,Qian Zhang,Liwen Xiao,Lysa Xiao*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 多轮LLM编程对话中存在回归积累问题，导致代码性能下降；验证门机制能有效缓解这一问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多轮LLM辅助编程中，后续代码可能破坏先前需求，需系统研究回归积累现象及其解决方案。

Method: 基于HumanEval+和MBPP+构建542个8轮需求演化任务，评估6个LLM共26,016个轮次实例，分析回归错误并构建分类法，测试验证门策略。

Result: 所有模型均出现回归积累（40%-73%任务丢失正确行为），跨轮冲突为主因；验证门将DeepSeek-V3最终轮质量从75.8%提至87.9%，Llama-3.1-8B从31.6%提至47.3%。

Conclusion: 单轮性能高估多轮可靠性，未来需关注需求保留及验证门机制。

中文摘要：在基于大型语言模型（LLM）的软件开发中，编码通常是迭代的。我们研究了多轮LLM编程对话中的回归积累问题，即后来的代码建议可能破坏早期引入的需求。因此，可靠性不仅取决于满足当前请求，还取决于保留先前满足的行为。我们构建了来自HumanEval+和MBPP+的542个任务，并将每个任务扩展为一个8轮的需求演化链。我们在26,016个轮次实例（542 x 6 x 8）上评估了六个LLM。在每一轮，我们测试当前代码是否仍通过早期基准测试。我们还从失败群体中分析了384个失败案例，并通过独立四标注者标注构建了多轮回归错误的分类法。我们的结果表明，所有六个模型都出现了回归积累：40%到73%的任务在整个对话中丢失了先前正确的行为。所有模型的最终轮质量均低于初始轮质量，尤其是当后续轮次添加输入验证或更广泛的输入类型时。人工分析表明，跨轮冲突（即后续代码与早期需求冲突）是主要的失败类别。我们进一步发现，验证门机制（检查新代码是否通过先前测试并触发回滚和重试）是唯一能持续改进所有模型的策略，将DeepSeek-V3的最终轮质量从75.8%提高到87.9%，将Llama-3.1-8B的最终轮质量从31.6%提高到47.3%。这些发现表明，强大的单轮性能可能高估多轮编程对话中的可靠性。未来的评估和工具设计应测试后续代码建议是否保留早期需求，并应包括验证门机制。

Original abstract: In LLM-assisted software development, coding is often iterative. We study regression accumulation in multi-turn LLM programming conversations, where later code suggestions may break requirements introduced in earlier turns. Reliability therefore depends not only on satisfying the current request, but also on preserving previously satisfied behavior.
  We construct 542 tasks from HumanEval+ and MBPP+ and extend each task into an 8-turn requirement-evolution chain. We evaluate six LLMs on 26,016 turn instances (542 x 6 x 8). At each turn, we test whether the current code still passes earlier benchmark tests. We also analyze 384 failure cases from the failure population and build a taxonomy of multi-turn regression bugs through independent four-annotator labeling.
  Our results show that regression accumulation appears across all six models: 40% to 73% of tasks lose previously correct behavior over the full conversation. Final-turn quality is lower than initial-turn quality across models, especially when later turns add input validation or broader input types. Manual analysis shows that Cross-Turn Conflict, where later code conflicts with earlier requirements, is the main failure class. We further find that Verification Gate, which checks new code against prior tests and triggers rollback and retry, is the only strategy that consistently improves all models, raising final-turn quality from 75.8% to 87.9% on DeepSeek-V3 and from 31.6% to 47.3% on Llama-3.1-8B.
  These findings suggest that strong single-turn performance can overestimate reliability in multi-turn coding conversations. Future evaluation and tool design should test whether later code suggestions preserve earlier requirements and should include Verification Gate mechanisms.

</details>


### [12] [An Exploratory Study on LLM-Generated Code and Comments in Code Repositories](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01867v1)
*Yongyi Ji,Jiaji Wang,Yi Zhou,Fuxiang Chen,Hongji Yang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过检测器代理分析，研究了2011-2015年间公司和社区维护仓库中LLM生成的代码与注释的特征，发现LLM生成代码随时间减少，多见于测试用例，且公司仓库中比例更高，但仅少数错误与之相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决对LLM生成代码与注释在实际使用中的疑虑，尤其是调试时间增加和注释不自然的问题，并探究其在不同类型仓库中的分布及与错误的关系。

Method: 使用多种检测工具和技术，对2021至2025年间活跃的公司维护和社区维护仓库进行代理分析，检测可能由LLM生成的代码和注释。

Result: 被检测为LLM生成的代码随时间减少，且频繁出现在测试用例中；注释稳定；代码存在大量仓库内克隆，注释语法正确率低；公司仓库中LLM生成比例更高；仅少数人工标记错误与LLM生成代码相关。

Conclusion: LLM生成代码在仓库中呈下降趋势，多用于测试，且与错误关联性低；公司仓库更倾向使用；注释质量仍需提升。

中文摘要：LLM在软件开发中的使用在代码生成和摘要等任务上日益广泛。大型科技公司的报告显示，其约20%至30%的代码是由LLM生成的。然而，人们对于LLM生成的代码和注释的实际使用仍存在怀疑，例如对调试生成代码需花费更多时间以及生成注释的不自然性的担忧。在本文中，我们研究了被检测为可能由LLM生成的代码和注释及其特征、公司维护与社区维护仓库之间的差异，以及错误与LLM生成代码关联的可能性。我们使用多种工具和技术对2021年至2025年间活跃的公司维护和社区维护仓库进行了广泛实验，这些工具和技术可检测由LLM生成的代码和注释。基于检测器代理分析，结果表明，被检测为可能由LLM生成的代码随时间推移而减少，并频繁出现在测试用例中，而注释则相对稳定。代理结果进一步表明，被检测为可能由LLM生成的代码显示出大量的仓库内部代码克隆，而注释中语法正确的句子比例较低。此外，公司维护的仓库中被检测为可能由LLM生成的代码和注释的比例更高，并且只有一小部分人工标记的错误被检测为可能与LLM生成的代码相关。

Original abstract: The use of LLMs in software development has become increasingly widespread on tasks such as code generation and summarization. Reports from large technology companies showed that around 20% to 30% of their code are generated by LLMs. However, there remains skepticism about the practical usage of LLM-generated code and comments, such as concerns on more time for debugging the generated code and the unnaturalness of the generated comments. In this paper, we study the code and comments detected as likely to be generated by LLMs and their characteristics, the differences between company- and community-maintained repositories, and how likely bugs are associated with LLM-generated code. We conduct extensive experiments on active company- and community-maintained repositories from 2021 to 2025 using various tools and techniques that detect code and comments generated by LLMs. Based on our detector-based proxy analysis, the results suggest that code detected as likely to be generated by LLMs decreased over time and appeared frequently in test cases, while that of comments remains relatively stable. Proxy results further suggest that code detected as likely to be generated by LLMs shows substantial intra-repository code clones, whereas comments exhibit a relatively low proportion of grammatically correct sentences. In addition, the company-maintained repositories show a higher percentage of code and comments detected as likely to be generated by LLMs, and only a small percentage of the human-labelled bugs are detected as being likely associated with LLM-generated code.

### [13] [Understanding Build Reproducibility in the F-Droid Ecosystem](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01890v1)
*Denise Nanni,Julien Malka,Stefano Zacchiroli,Théo Zimmermann,Gabriele d'Angelo*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 对F-Droid应用的实证研究发现，逐比特可重现率随时间上升，但可重建性随时间衰减，缺失依赖是主要失败原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: F-Droid在应用发布时测试可重现性，但无法保证未来持续成立，软件生态系统演变可能导致可重现性下降，影响软件保存和安全性。

Method: 分析F-Droid历史可重现性日志，并尝试重建18,904个先前可重现的应用版本，评估重建成功率和逐比特可重现性。

Result: 整体可重现率随时间上升；重建成功率为83%，其中缺失依赖占失败的76%；成功重建的应用中94%仍可逐比特重现。

Conclusion: 逐比特可重现性在可重建的应用中基本保持，但可重建性本身高度敏感于时间衰减。

中文摘要：开源应用程序的安全性在很大程度上受益于从源代码重建并验证输出的可能性。F-Droid是一个著名的开源Android应用程序发行平台，它在应用发布时系统性地从源代码重建应用，并测试其逐比特可重现性。然而，F-Droid无法保证应用的可重现性在未来持续成立。随着软件生态系统的演变，可重现性可能下降，对软件保存和安全性产生潜在负面影响。我们首次对F-Droid应用生态系统中的构建可重现性进行了实证研究。通过分析历史可重现性日志，我们发现整体逐比特可重现率随时间稳步上升（随着新版本应用的发布）。然后，我们通过尝试重建F-Droid先前确认为逐比特可重现的18,904个应用版本（发布于2018年9月至2026年2月之间），评估了固定版本应用的可重现性随时间的变化，实现了83%的重建成功率，并确定缺失依赖是失败的主要原因，占不可重建案例的76%。在成功重建的应用中，94%也是逐比特可重现的——即重建后仍产生逐比特相同的工件。这些结果共同表明，虽然逐比特可重现性在可重建的应用中基本保持，但可重建性本身对时间衰减高度敏感。

Original abstract: The security of open source applications benefits considerably from the possibility of rebuilding their source and verifying the output. F-Droid, a prominent distribution for open source Android applications, systematically rebuilds them from source and tests their bitwise reproducibility at app publishing time. However, F-Droid offers no guarantee that app reproducibility will continue to hold in the future. As software ecosystems evolve, reproducibility may degrade, with potential negative consequences for software preservation and security. We present the first empirical study of build reproducibility in the F-Droid app ecosystem. Analyzing historical reproducibility logs, we find that the overall bitwise reproducibility rate has been steadily increasing over time (as new versions of apps are published). We then evaluate how reproducibility holds in time for fixed app versions, by attempting to rebuild 18 904 app versions that F-Droid had previously confirmed bitwise reproducible, published between September 2018 and February 2026, achieving an 83% rebuild success rate, and identify missing dependencies as the dominant cause of failure, accounting for 76% of non-rebuildable cases. Among successfully rebuilt apps, 94% are also bitwise reproducible-i.e., they still yield bitwise identical artifacts upon rebuild. Together, these results show that while bitwise reproducibility largely holds for apps that can be rebuilt, rebuildability itself is highly sensitive to temporal decay.

### [14] [AI Writes Faster Than Humans Can Review: A Longitudinal Study of an Enterprise 2x Mandate](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01904v1)
*Hao He,Shyam Agarwal,Yegor Denisov-Blanch,Pavel Azaletskiy,Sanmi Koyejo,Bogdan Vasilescu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 一项关于企业强制使用AI编码工具的纵向案例研究显示，人均拉取请求吞吐量最终翻倍（2.09倍），通过交错双重差分法将收益与AI采用和使用联系起来，强制要求起催化剂作用。收益广泛共享但集中于新代码，并重构了代码审查自动化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺乏关于企业强制使用AI编码工具后生产力变化的纵向证据。

Method: 对一家中型AI前沿公司进行定量案例研究，使用802名开发者和196,212个拉取请求的面板数据，采用交错双重差分设计分析强制要求对AI采用及生产力的影响。

Result: 人均吞吐量达到强制前的2.09倍；收益主要归因于AI采用和累积使用，而非强制要求本身；收益广泛但集中于新代码；自动化审查覆盖人类审查，审阅者负载翻倍，合并与回滚率稳定。

Conclusion: 强制使用AI编码工具通过促进采用和使用显著提升生产力，但收益并非直接来自强制，且对代码审查过程产生了结构性影响。

中文摘要：企业越来越多地强制要求使用AI编码工具，并报告了巨大的生产力提升，然而关于这种强制要求如何展开的纵向证据却很少。在本文中，我们提出了一个关于记录在案的“2倍”强制要求的定量案例研究，该案例发生在一家中型、AI前沿的公司，自2025年年中以来，该公司一直致力于将每名工程师的合并拉取请求数量翻倍。在802名开发者和196,212个拉取请求（2024年1月至2026年4月）的面板数据中，人均吞吐量最终翻倍，于2026年4月达到强制前基线的2.09倍，据我们所知，这是AI编码工具现场部署报告中最大的收益之一。一个交错的双重差分设计将这种收益中开发者内部的部分与AI采用联系起来，并且随着累积使用量的增加收益进一步增长，而强制要求则充当催化剂而非直接驱动因素。由于采用和使用强度并非随机分配，我们将这一证据解读为强烈暗示了一个采用和使用渠道，而非精确的因果归因。收益在不同资历级别中广泛共享，但集中在新代码中，并且不能跨模型世代分离。采用还围绕自动化重构了代码审查：每位审阅者的负载大约翻倍，自动化审查超过了人类审查，而合并和回滚率保持稳定。

Original abstract: Enterprises increasingly mandate AI coding tools and report large productivity gains, yet longitudinal evidence on how such a mandate unfolds is scarce. In this paper, we present a quantitative case study of a documented enterprise "2x" mandate at a mid-sized, AI-forward company that has been committed to doubling merged pull requests per engineer since mid-2025. In a panel of 802 developers and 196,212 pull requests (January 2024-April 2026), per-capita throughput eventually doubled, reaching 2.09x the pre-mandate baseline in April 2026, among the largest gains reported from a field deployment of AI coding tools to our knowledge. A staggered difference-in-differences design links the within-developer share of this gain to AI adoption and to a further gain that grows with accumulated use, with the mandate acting as a catalyst rather than a direct driver. Because adoption and usage intensity were not randomly assigned, we read this evidence as strongly implicating an adoption-and-use channel rather than as exact causal attribution. The gain is broadly shared across seniority yet concentrated in newer code and not separable across model generations. Adoption also restructured code review around automation: per-reviewer load roughly doubled and automated review overtook human review, while merge and revert rates held steady.

### [15] [Beyond Textual Repository Exploration: Dual-Modal Structural Reasoning for Agentic Issue Resolution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01929v1)
*Jiayi Zhang,Kai Huang,Yang Liu,Chunyang Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: DUALVIEW通过引入双模态结构脚手架和视觉推理，显著提升了智能体在长视界仓库中的问题解决性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖顺序文本导航，难以处理大规模仓库的长程依赖，导致探索漂移和不完全定位。

Method: DUALVIEW构建四个互补图视图（MCG、FCG、CHG、PDG），并通过可查询接口暴露视觉和文本响应，使智能体能直接推理持久视觉表示。

Result: 在SWE-bench Pro和Verified上，DUALVIEW一致提升了问题解决性能；消融实验表明增益来自文本结构信息和视觉外部化。

Conclusion: DUALVIEW通过视觉推理增强仓库探索，有效支持长视界代码库的探索与修复。

中文摘要：近期在智能体程序修复方面的进展通过迭代仓库探索显著提升了问题解决能力。然而，现有方法主要依赖于顺序的、基于文本的代码导航，这从根本上限制了它们在具有复杂和长程依赖关系的大规模、长视界仓库中进行推理的能力。当问题解决智能体通过碎片化的文本观察遍历仓库时，结构信息（如模块组织、调用关系和依赖链）必须在交互步骤中反复重建，常常导致探索漂移和不完整的定位。我们提出了DUALVIEW，一个双模态结构脚手架框架，将视觉推理引入问题解决智能体的仓库探索中。DUALVIEW通过四种互补的图视图来表示仓库结构：模块耦合图（MCG）、函数调用图（FCG）、类层次图（CHG）和程序依赖图（PDG），并通过一个可查询的界面暴露视觉和文本响应。智能体无需从一系列文本观察中重建仓库结构，而是可以直接推理代码依赖的持久视觉表示，从而更有效地探索和理解长视界代码库。我们在SWE-bench Pro和Verified上评估了DUALVIEW。结果表明，DUALVIEW在不同智能体架构和模型系列中一致地提升了问题解决性能。进一步的消融研究表明，这些提升不仅来自文本结构信息，还来自仓库依赖的视觉外化，后者更好地支持了长视界仓库探索。

Original abstract: Recent advances in agentic program repair have significantly improved issue resolution by enabling iterative repository exploration. However, existing approaches predominantly rely on sequential, text-based code navigation, which fundamentally limits their ability to reason over large-scale long-horizon repositories with complex and long-range dependencies. As issue-resolution agents traverse repositories through fragmented textual observations, structural information such as module organization, call relationships, and dependency chains must be repeatedly reconstructed across interaction steps, often leading to exploration drift and incomplete localization. We present DUALVIEW, a dual-modal structural scaffolding framework that brings visual reasoning into repository exploration for issue-resolution agents. DUALVIEW represents repository structure through four complementary graph views: Module Coupling Graph (MCG), Function Call Graph (FCG), Class Hierarchy Graph (CHG), and Program Dependence Graph (PDG), and exposes them through a queryable interface with visual and textual responses. Rather than reconstructing repository structure from a sequence of textual observations, agents can directly reason over persistent visual representations of code dependencies, enabling more effective exploration and understanding of long-horizon codebases. We evaluate DUALVIEW on SWE-bench Pro and Verified. Results show that DUALVIEW consistently improves issue-resolution performance across different agent architectures and model families. Further ablation studies demonstrate that the gains arise not only from textual structural information but also from visual externalization of repository dependencies, which better supports long-horizon repository exploration.

</details>


### [16] [Underspecification does not imply Incoherence: The Risks of Semantic Collapse in Coding Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01953v1)
*Cedric Richter,Mike Papadakis*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文发现LLM在任务描述模糊时常坍缩到单一错误解释，产生一致但行为失调的代码（有害语义坍缩），在多个代码生成基准中普遍存在，且现有依赖不一致性的技术存在盲点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战“提示未充分指定会导致不一致性”的常见假设，揭示LLM在模糊任务描述下的真实失败模式。

Method: 分析LLM在MBPP、HumanEval、LiveCodeBench等基准上生成代码的一致性，并通过故意注入模糊性测量有害语义坍缩的比率。

Result: 有害语义坍缩影响MBPP中10%+、HumanEval中3%、LiveCodeBench中32%的任务；注入模糊性后比率提升5倍以上。

Conclusion: 当前依赖不一致性作为模糊性代理的消歧和正确性估计技术存在根本盲点，需要新的方法处理提示未充分指定问题。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在任务描述清晰精确时，生成代码的能力日益增强。然而，在实践中，用户提供的任务描述往往模糊、不完整或矛盾，导致预期程序行为的关键方面未得到充分指定。在这种情况下，多个行为上不同的解释可能同样满足描述，但在语义上存在差异，这些差异会影响用户意图。研究人员通常假设，提示未充分指定会表现为不一致性：当多次询问时，LLM会生成多个语义不同的实现，反映任务描述的模糊性。在本文中，我们挑战了这一假设。我们发现，LLM经常坍缩到任务描述的单一错误解释上，一致地生成连贯但行为失调的代码。我们将这种失败模式称为“有害语义坍缩”，并发现它影响了MBPP中超过10%的任务、HumanEval中3%的任务以及LiveCodeBench中32%的任务，这些基准都被认为是良好指定的。通过故意在基准提示中注入未充分指定问题，该比率上升到5倍以上，暴露了依赖于不一致性作为提示未充分指定代理的消歧和正确性估计技术中的根本盲点。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have become increasingly effective at generating code when task descriptions are clear and precise. Yet, in practice, user-provided task descriptions are often ambiguous, incomplete, or contradictory, leaving critical aspects of the intended program behavior underspecified. In such cases, multiple behaviorally distinct interpretations may satisfy the description equally well, yet semantically differ in ways that matter/affect the user intent. A natural expectation, often assumed by researchers, is that prompt underspecification manifests as incoherence: When asked multiple times, an LLM produces multiple semantically distinct implementations reflecting the ambiguity of the task description. In this paper, we challenge this assumption. We find that LLMs frequently collapse onto a single incorrect interpretation of the task description, consistently generating coherent but behaviorally misaligned code. We term this failure mode detrimental semantic collapse and find that it affects over 10% of tasks in MBPP, 3% in HumanEval, and 32% of LiveCodeBench, all benchmarks assumed to be well-specified. By deliberately injecting underspecification issues in the benchmark prompts, the rate rises to over 5 times, exposing a fundamental blind spot in disambiguation and correctness estimation techniques that rely on incoherence as a proxy for prompt underspecification.

</details>


### [17] [Epic-Organized vs. Requirement-Aligned Gherkin: An Empirical Evaluation of LLM-Based Acceptance Criteria Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01980v1)
*Shahbaz Siddeeq,Mateen Abbasi,Jussi Rasku,Zheying Zhang,François Christophe,Tommi Mikkonen,Pekka Abrahamsson*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究比较了史诗组织与需求对齐的LLM生成Gherkin场景，结果表明史诗组织策略在正确性、可执行性和完整性上更优，且语义覆盖率相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动化编写BDD验收标准仍是需求工程中的手动瓶颈，需要改进生成方法以提高质量和覆盖率。

Method: 使用Timeless（史诗组织LLM流水线）与零样本基线，在PURE数据集（4个需求文档，107个需求）上比较，通过结构有效性、TF-IDF和稠密嵌入的语义覆盖率以及四位研究人员的盲审专家评估进行评价。

Result: JSON约束流水线100%结构有效，基线99%；语义覆盖率Timeless 94.3% vs 基线92.9%；专家评分上，正确性4.61 vs 4.14，可执行性4.61 vs 4.07，完整性4.31 vs 3.50，均偏好史诗组织。

Conclusion: 史诗组织的LLM生成可以在保持相当语义覆盖率的同时提高感知的Gherkin质量，但需要更广泛的重复研究来验证泛化性。

中文摘要：Gherkin行为驱动开发（BDD）验收标准的自动编写仍然是需求工程中的一个手动瓶颈。本研究调查了基于史诗组织的LLM生成的Gherkin是否比基于需求对齐的生成具有更高质量和覆盖率。我们将我们的Timeless（一种基于史诗组织的LLM流水线）方法与一个朴素的大语言模型（LLM）基线在来自PURE数据集的四个需求文档（107个需求）上进行比较。评估涵盖结构指标、通过TF-IDF和稠密嵌入的自动化需求覆盖率，以及四位研究人员的盲审专家评估。在我们的评估中，JSON约束的流水线在所有生成的输出上都产生了结构有效的场景，而零样本基线达到了99%的结构有效性。语义覆盖率与基线相当，Timeless达到了94.3%的语义需求覆盖率，而基线为92.9%。TF-IDF对史诗组织输出的覆盖率得分较低，表明当场景以更高抽象级别改写需求时，词汇指标可能遗漏覆盖率。专家评估者更偏好史诗组织策略在正确性（4.61对4.14）、可执行性（4.61对4.07）和完整性（4.31对3.50）方面。总体而言，结果表明史诗组织的生成可以在保持相当语义覆盖率的同时提高感知的Gherkin质量，尽管在推广这一发现之前需要更广泛的重复研究。

Original abstract: Automated authoring of Gherkin Behavior-Driven Development (BDD) acceptance criteria remains a manual bottleneck in requirements engineering. This study investigates whether epic-organized LLM-generated Gherkin produces higher quality and coverage than requirement-aligned generation. We compare our Timeless (an epic-organized LLM pipeline) approach against a naive large language model (LLM) baseline on four requirements documents (107 requirements) from the PURE dataset. Evaluation covers structural metrics, automated requirement coverage via TF-IDF and dense embeddings, and blind expert assessment by four researchers. In our evaluation, the JSON-constrained pipeline produced structurally valid scenarios across all generated outputs, while the zero-shot baseline achieved 99% structural validity. Semantic coverage was comparable to the baseline, with Timeless achieving 94.3% semantic Requirement Coverage Rate compared with 92.9% for the baseline. TF-IDF produced lower coverage scores for the epic-organized output, suggesting that lexical metrics may miss coverage when scenarios paraphrase requirements at a higher level of abstraction. Expert raters prefer the epic-organized strategy on Correctness (4.61 vs 4.14), Executability (4.61 vs 4.07), and Completeness (4.31 vs 3.50). Overall, the results suggest that epic-organized generation can improve perceived Gherkin quality while maintaining comparable semantic coverage, although broader replication is needed before generalizing this finding.

</details>


### [18] [Benchmarking Quantum Software Testing with Scalable Quantum Programs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02029v1)
*Yuechen Li,Minqi Shao,Xiyuan Li,Jianjun Zhao,Kai-Yuan Cai*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了Qolumbina基准，包含40个可测试量子程序，用于量子软件测试的受控实验，支持可扩展性和后端效应分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子软件测试研究缺乏包含可测试、可扩展且反映实际开发实践的程序的基准，导致公平比较和可重复性受限。

Method: 从开源存储库中精选40个程序，通过系统选择、重构、规范、测试用例示例、单元测试和标准化接口转化为测试主体，并定义面向QST的表征标准。

Result: 实证表明Qolumbina覆盖多样测试属性并支持可扩展性分析；通过对比实验验证了其在执行成本和故障检测研究中的可行性，并发现后端依赖效应。

Conclusion: Qolumbina为量子软件测试提供了有效基准，有助于标准化评估和发现后端相关影响，未来可进一步扩展程序规模和多样性。

中文摘要：量子软件测试（QST）检查量子程序是否按照其预期规范运行。QST研究的一个关键需求是支持对可测试且更能反映当前软件开发实践的程序进行严格经验评估的基准。然而，现有研究严重依赖小型硬编码或电路级基准，而可用的量子程序分散在存储库中，没有明确的选择标准，这限制了公平比较和系统可重复性。为此，我们提出了Qolumbina，一个用于可控QST实验的可扩展量子程序基准基础设施。Qolumbina从开源存储库中精选了40个程序，通过系统选择、重构、规范、测试用例示例、单元测试和标准化接口将其转化为可测试主体。我们还提出了面向QST的标准来根据功能、输出行为、开发复杂性和量子特定执行复杂性表征量子程序。使用这些标准，我们的实证研究表明Qolumbina覆盖了多样化的测试相关属性，并支持超出固定大小电路基准的可扩展性分析。通过与两种近期QST方法的受控实验，我们展示了使用Qolumbina进行执行成本和故障检测研究的可行性，并强调了可能影响QST结果解释的后端相关效应。

Original abstract: Quantum software testing (QST) checks whether quantum programs behave according to their intended specifications. A key requirement for QST research is a benchmark that supports rigorous empirical evaluation on programs that are testable and better reflect current software development practices. However, existing studies heavily rely on small hard-coded or circuit-level benchmarks, while available quantum programs are scattered across repositories without clear selection criteria, which limits fair comparison and systematic reproducibility. To this end, we present Qolumbina, a benchmark infrastructure for controlled QST experiments on scalable quantum programs. Qolumbina curates 40 programs from open-source repositories, turns them into test-ready subjects through systematic selection, refactoring, specifications, test case examples, unit tests, and standardized interfaces. We also propose QST-oriented criteria to characterize quantum programs along functionality, output behavior, development complexity, and quantum-specific execution complexity. Using these criteria, our empirical study shows that Qolumbina covers diverse testing-relevant properties and supports scalability analysis beyond fixed-size circuit benchmarks. Through controlled experiments with two recent QST approaches, we demonstrate the feasibility of using Qolumbina for execution-cost and fault-detection studies, and highlight backend-dependent effects that can influence QST result interpretation.

### [19] [Mitigating Package Hallucinations in Large Language Models via Model Editing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02052v1)
*Shuhan Liu,Yukai Zhao,Xing Hu,Kui Liu,Xiaohu Yang,Xin Xia*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: BOUND是一个轻量级局部模型编辑框架，通过风险感知定位和边界感知目标函数减少LLM中的包幻觉，在多项任务中显著降低包级幻觉率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在软件工程任务中常产生包幻觉，生成无效或不存在包名，可被利用于供应链攻击，因此需要缓解包幻觉以提高可靠性和安全性。

Method: 提出BOUND框架，将包幻觉缓解视为包有效性边界编辑问题：先通过风险感知定位策略找到相关模块，再使用边界感知目标函数（强化有效包、抑制幻觉包、保持局部行为）编辑模块（轻量LoRA适配器）。

Result: 包推荐任务中Package-HR降低79.9%（编辑提示）和65.4%（未见提示）；代码生成中降低12.8%，pip install推荐中降低34.0%。

Conclusion: BOUND有效细化了LLM的包有效性边界，在减少幻觉的同时保持推荐能力，并泛化到多种包相关任务，提升了输出可靠性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在软件工程任务中展现了强大的能力，例如代码生成、库推荐和依赖配置。然而，最近的研究表明，LLM可能会遭受包幻觉问题，即生成不存在或无效的包名。这些幻觉可能被利用于软件供应链攻击，因为攻击者可能以幻觉名称注册恶意包。因此，缓解包幻觉对于提高LLM辅助软件开发的可靠性和安全性至关重要。在本文中，我们介绍了BOUND，一个轻量级的局部模型编辑框架，用于缓解LLM中的包幻觉。BOUND将包幻觉缓解形式化为一个包有效性边界编辑问题，其中边界指的是模型在给定任务上下文中区分有效包和幻觉包名的能力。它首先通过风险感知定位策略定位与包幻觉相关的模块，然后使用边界感知的目标函数编辑这些模块，该目标函数强化有效包、抑制幻觉包并保持局部行为。实验结果表明，BOUND有效地减少了包幻觉，同时保持了有效的包推荐。在包推荐任务中，BOUND在编辑提示上将包级幻觉率（Package-HR）降低了79.9%，在未见提示上降低了65.4%。学习到的包有效性边界进一步泛化到其他包相关任务，在代码生成中将Package-HR降低了12.8%，在pip install推荐中降低了34.0%。这些结果表明，BOUND细化了LLM的包有效性边界，并提高了包相关输出的可靠性。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong capabilities in software engineering tasks, such as code generation, library recommendation, and dependency configuration. However, recent studies show that LLMs may suffer from package hallucination, where they generate non-existent or invalid package names. These hallucinations can be exploited in software supply chain attacks, as attackers may register malicious packages under hallucinated names. Therefore, mitigating package hallucination is important for improving the reliability and security of LLM-assisted software development. In this paper, we introduce BOUND, a lightweight localized model editing framework for mitigating package hallucinations in LLMs. BOUND formulates package hallucination mitigation as a package-validity boundary editing problem, where the boundary refers to the model's ability to distinguish valid packages from hallucinated package names under a given task context. It first locates modules related to package hallucination through a risk-aware localization strategy, and then edits these modules with lightweight LoRA adapters using a boundary-aware objective that reinforces valid packages, suppresses hallucinated packages, and preserves locality behavior. Experimental results show that BOUND effectively reduces package hallucinations while preserving valid package recommendations. In the package recommendation task, BOUND reduces package-level hallucination rate (Package-HR) by 79.9% on edit prompts and by 65.4% on unseen prompts. The learned package-validity boundary further generalizes to other package-related tasks, reducing Package-HR by 12.8% in code generation and by 34.0% in pip install recommendation. These results show that BOUND refines the package-validity boundary of LLMs and improves the reliability of package-related outputs.

</details>


### [20] [Prompt Coverage Adequacy](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02057v1)
*Florian Tambon,Michael Konstantinou,Cedric Richter,Charles Chenouard,Mark Harman,Mike Papadakis*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出提示覆盖充分性准则，利用LLM注意力机制度量测试对提示需求的覆盖，比传统代码覆盖多发现30%以上故障。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM和自主代理将软件开发抽象层次提升到意图表达，提示成为主要开发工件，传统代码覆盖无法有效指导测试，需要新的覆盖准则。

Method: 基于注意力增强，在提示层面利用LLM注意力机制计算提示覆盖充分性，评估其与故障检测的关系及测试生成效果。

Result: 提示覆盖与故障检测有效性相关，在测试生成中比传统代码覆盖多发现30%以上故障。

Conclusion: 提示覆盖充分性可作为LLM驱动软件开发中测试度量的基础，弥补经典覆盖准则的不足。

中文摘要：近年来，越来越明显的是，大型语言模型（LLMs）和自主代理通过将重点从编写精确过程转向表达意图和目标，提高了软件开发的抽象层次。这种范式转变带来了新的挑战，特别是在测试应如何指导方面，当提示（而非代码）成为主要开发工件时。为了应对这一挑战，我们提出了提示覆盖充分性，这是一种新颖的覆盖准则，旨在支持对从任务描述生成的代码进行测试。提示覆盖充分性类似于传统代码覆盖，但它在LLM和基于代理的编程中使用的提示层面运作。具体来说，它通过利用LLM的注意力机制来度量给定测试套件满足提示中表达的需求的程度。我们基于注意力增强，在两个数据集和多个LLM上评估了该准则的一个简单实例。我们的结果表明，提示覆盖与故障检测有效性相关，并且在用于指导测试生成时，可以比传统代码覆盖发现多30%以上的故障。这些发现表明，提示覆盖充分性可以作为开发更适合新兴LLM驱动软件开发范式的测试度量的基础，解决了经典覆盖准则在这种新背景下的局限性。

Original abstract: In recent years, it has become increasingly evident that large language models (LLMs) and autonomous agents raise the level of abstraction in software development by shifting the focus from writing precise procedures to expressing intents and goals. This paradigm shift introduces new challenges, particularly in how testing should be guided when prompts, rather than code, become primary development artifacts. To address this challenge, we propose Prompt Coverage Adequacy, a novel coverage criterion designed to support the testing of code generated from task descriptions. Prompt Coverage Adequacy serves as an analog to traditional code coverage, but operates at the level of prompts used in LLM and agent-based programming. Specifically, it measures how well a given test suite satisfies the requirements expressed in a prompt by leveraging the attention mechanisms of LLMs. We evaluate a simple instantiation of this criterion, based on attention boosting, across two datasets and multiple LLMs. Our results demonstrate that Prompt Coverage is associated with fault-detection effectiveness and can uncover over 30+% more faults than traditional code coverage when used to guide test generation. These findings suggest that Prompt Coverage Adequacy can serve as a foundation for developing testing metrics better suited to the emerging paradigm of LLM-driven software development, addressing the limitations of classical coverage criteria in this new context.

</details>


### [21] [File-Level Copying Is an Implicit Dependency in Open Source](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02059v1)
*Runzhi He,Audris Mockus,Wenhao Yang,Minghui Zhou*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过分析整个开源生态系统的文件级复制行为，发现未管理的软件复用导致供应链可见性严重缺失，安全风险和许可证风险集中在特定的复制形式中，且现有依赖扫描器无法检测到这些风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 文件级复制是一种广泛存在但不受管理的软件复用形式，它会移除包管理器提供的依赖项信号（来源、维护、安全性、合规性），降低供应链可见性。需要刻画这种未管理复用的规模和后果。

Method: 使用World of Code（WoC）进行混合方法研究，从0.1%的提交样本中提取690,500个复制事件，保留3,912个包含意图标签的理性复制提交，并分析13种轴向复制形式的意图、过时程度、来源记录以及安全/许可证风险集中情况。

Result: 发现13种复制形式不能可靠代表开发者意图；复制源代码常过时（中位数155天），很少记录来源（4.3%）和版本（2.0%）；安全风险集中在供应商依赖（88%的CVE风险提交），许可证风险集中在直接源代码复用（66%的候选）；两者均影响打包软件且对声明元数据扫描器不可见。

Conclusion: 文件级复制导致的可见性缺口具有形式特异性，且现有依赖扫描器无法检测到由此引入的安全和许可证风险，表明需要更完善的机制来恢复供应链可见性。

中文摘要：文件级复制是一种广泛存在但不受管理的软件复用形式。跨仓库复制文件降低了供应链可见性：它移除了包管理器为声明的依赖项提供的四个可观察信号（来源、维护、安全性和合规性），且没有恢复这些信号的机制。为了刻画这种未管理复用的规模和后果，我们使用World of Code（WoC）对整个开源生态系统中的复制行为进行了混合方法研究。从0.1%的提交样本中，我们提取了690,500个复制事件，并保留了3,912个包含意图标签的理性复制提交。我们发现，涵盖供应商依赖、硬件/驱动同步、脚手架、UI资源和直接源代码复用的13种轴向复制形式，并不能可靠地代表开发者意图：在包含理性的提交中，硬件/驱动复制主要是分支维护工作（78%），而依赖供应商复制更多意味着绕过上游（70%）而非离线可用性。这些可见性缺口具有形式特异性：安全性和许可证风险集中在互补的复制形式中。复制的源代码经常过时（中位数155天；38.5%超过一年），且很少记录可恢复的来源（4.3%有文档），更不用说可检查的版本（2.0%有版本标记）；即使是供应商复制的依赖，也只有10%的时间记录了来源。安全风险集中在供应商依赖中：在整个WoC图中，有17,314个CVE风险复制提交，88%属于依赖供应商形式；80%的CVSS评分>=7.0，且上游修复采用率仅为47%-84%。许可证风险集中在直接源代码复用中：有41,777个预验证候选，66%属于源代码形式，其中39个经验证的高星级违规（kappa=0.752）。这两种风险都会传播到打包的软件中，且仅基于声明元数据的依赖扫描器无法检测到它们。

Original abstract: File-level copying is a widespread but ungoverned form of software reuse. Copying files across repositories reduces supply-chain visibility: it removes the four observable signals a package manager provides for a declared dependency (provenance, maintenance, security, and compliance) with no mechanism to restore them. To characterize the scale and consequences of this unmanaged reuse, we present a mixed-method study of copying across the entire open-source ecosystem using World of Code (WoC). From a 0.1% commit sample, we extract 690,500 copy events and retain 3,912 rationale-bearing copy commits for intent labeling. We show that the 13 axial copy forms, spanning vendored dependencies, hardware/driver synchronization, scaffolding, UI assets, and direct source-code reuse, are unreliable proxies for developer intent: among rationale-bearing commits, hardware/driver copies are predominantly fork-maintenance work (78%), while dependency-vendoring copies more often signal upstream bypass (70%) than offline availability. These visibility gaps are form-specific: security and license risk concentrate in complementary copy forms. Copied sources are frequently stale (median 155 days; 38.5% over one year old) and seldom record a recoverable origin (4.3% documented), let alone a checkable version (2.0% versioned); even vendored copies record where they came from only 10% of the time. Security risk concentrates in vendored dependencies: 17,314 CVE-risk copy commits in the full-WoC graph, 88% in the dependency-vendoring form; 80% score CVSS >= 7.0 and upstream-fix adoption is only 47%-84%. License risk concentrates in direct source-code reuse: 41,777 pre-validation candidates, 66% in the source-code form, with 39 verified high-star violations (kappa = 0.752). Both risks reach packaged software and are invisible to dependency scanners operating on declared metadata alone.

</details>


### [22] [Schedulable Job-Level Dependencies for Cause-Effect Chains via Graph Neural Networks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02624v1)
*Silviu S. Craciunas,Christian Hakert,Jian-Jia Chen,Zdeněk Hanzálek,Paul Pop*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出首个基于机器学习的JLD合成方法，使用两级GNN和生成-验证架构，大幅降低合成时间并优于贪心算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有JLD合成方法不检查强制性和可调度性，且效率低下，需要新方法。

Method: 提出基于两级GNN和温度控制采样的JLD合成方法，并嵌入生成-验证架构，包含数据年龄检查器、EDF可行性检查器和系统级需求界限测试。

Result: 基于ML的生成器性能优于贪心算法，合成时间降低数个数量级。

Conclusion: 学习到的结构先验可有效替代指数级枚举，适用于此类实时调度问题。

中文摘要：现代汽车软件架构包含大量混合关键性功能，这些功能在共享多核平台上执行，具有严格的实时性和端到端时序要求。此类系统中的传感器到执行器数据传播通常通过具有最坏情况数据年龄预算的因果链来表达。作业级依赖关系（JLDs）已被引入，以提供一种与调度器无关的机制，用于独立于底层调度器来限制数据年龄。然而，现有的合成JLDs的方法并不检查生成的JLDs是否在具体调度策略下可强制实施或在系统级别上可联合调度。在本文中，我们提出了第一个基于机器学习的JLD合成方法，该方法围绕一个具有温度控制采样的两级图神经网络构建，学习连接因果链配置与其JLD解决方案的结构模式。由于学习到的输出可能并非构造上正确，我们将GNN嵌入到一个新颖的生成-验证架构中，其中包含一个安全的DP数据年龄检查器、一个每链EDF可行性检查器以及一个系统级需求界限测试，以接受或拒绝每个候选。我们表明，基于ML的生成器在性能上大幅优于原始的贪心启发式算法，同时实现了数个数量级的合成时间降低，证明了学习到的结构先验可以有效替代此类实时调度问题上的指数级传播树枚举。

Original abstract: Modern automotive software architectures comprise large sets of mixed-criticality functions executing on shared multi-core platforms with strict real-time and end-to-end timing requirements. Sensor-to-actuator data propagation in such systems is typically expressed via cause-effect chains with worst-case data-age budgets. Job-level dependencies (JLDs) have been introduced to provide a schedule-agnostic mechanism for bounding the data age independently of the underlying scheduler. The state-of-the-art methods for synthesizing JLDs, however, do not check whether the produced JLDs are enforceable under a concrete scheduling policy or jointly schedulable at the system level. In this paper we propose the first machine-learning-based JLD synthesis method, built around a two-level Graph Neural Network with temperature-controlled sampling that learns the structural patterns connecting cause-effect chain configurations to their JLD solutions. Since learned outputs may not be correct by construction, we embed the GNN in a novel Generate-and-Verify architecture in which a safe DP data-age checker, together with a per-chain EDF feasibility checker and a system-level demand-bound test, accept or reject each candidate. We show that the ML-based generator substantially outperforms the original greedy heuristic while achieving orders-of-magnitude lower synthesis time, demonstrating that learned structural priors can effectively replace exponential propagation-tree enumeration on this class of real-time scheduling problems.

</details>


### [23] [A large-scale dataset of Android applications and their SDK dependencies](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02627v1)
*Aurora Gori Savellini,Tiziano Squartini,Massimo Riccaboni*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个大规模数据集，将Android应用与其集成的第三方SDK关联，通过静态分析流水线检测246个SDK及99,722个应用，并公开了可重复研究的基础设施。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 第三方SDK在移动应用中广泛使用但信息不透明，缺乏大规模数据集来研究其依赖关系。

Method: 结合AndroZoo的APK和元数据与Exodus Privacy的SDK检测规则，实现可重复的静态分析流水线，通过代码级签名匹配检测SDK。

Result: 数据集包含334,719个应用版本、99,722个Android应用和246个第三方SDK，并附有应用和SDK的元数据。

Conclusion: 该数据集支持构建应用-SDK依赖网络和提供商分析，为研究第三方技术依赖、数据收集和隐私基础设施提供了可重复使用的基础设施。

中文摘要：移动应用程序（app）越来越依赖第三方软件开发工具包（SDK）来提供广告、分析、认证、崩溃报告和位置服务等功能。这些组件构成了移动生态系统中一个重要但往往隐藏的层。在这里，我们展示了一个大规模数据集，将Android应用程序与它们集成的第三方SDK联系起来。该数据集是通过将AndroZoo中的应用程序包文件（APK）和元数据与Exodus Privacy提供的SDK检测规则相结合而构建的。我们实现了一个可重复的静态分析流水线，该流水线下载APK，检查其编译代码，并通过代码级签名匹配检测SDK：发布的数据集包含334,719个独特的应用版本观察（关联到99,722个Android应用程序）和246个第三方SDK——包括应用级元数据（如类别、评论、文件大小、下载次数、评分）和SDK级元数据（如类别、代码根目录、代码版本、名称）。该数据集支持构建大规模的应用-SDK依赖网络及其在两层上的投影；此外，SDK被映射到其对应的运营公司，从而能够对移动生态系统中的技术集中度和上游控制进行提供商级别的分析。为了支持可重复研究，流水线和数据集已在GitHub和Zenodo上公开发布；更广泛地说，该项目为研究Android应用中的第三方技术依赖、数据收集能力和隐私基础设施提供了一个可重复使用的研究基础设施。

Original abstract: Mobile applications (apps) increasingly rely on third-party Software Development Kits (SDKs) to provide services such as advertising, analytics, authentication, crash reporting, and location services. These components form an important, but often hidden, layer of the mobile ecosystem. Here, we present a large-scale dataset linking Android apps to the third-party SDKs they integrate. The dataset was constructed by combining app package files (APKs) and metadata from AndroZoo with SDK detection rules provided by Exodus Privacy. We implemented a reproducible, static-analysis pipeline that downloads APKs, inspects their compiled code, and detects SDKs through code-level signature matching: the released dataset contains 334,719 unique app-version observations (associated with 99,722 Android apps) and 246 third-party SDKs - including app-level metadata such as categories, comments, file size, download counts, ratings and SDK-level metadata such as categories, code roots, code versions, names. The dataset supports the construction of a large-scale app-SDK dependency network and its projection onto both layers; in addition, SDKs are mapped to their corresponding operating companies, enabling provider-level analysis of technological concentration and upstream control in the mobile ecosystem. To support reproducible research, the pipeline and dataset are publicly released on GitHub and Zenodo; more broadly, the project provides a reusable research infrastructure for studying third-party technological dependencies, data-collection capabilities, and privacy infrastructures across Android apps.

### [24] [Coding Agents Are Guessing: Measuring Action-Boundary Violations in Underspecified DevOps Instructions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02294v1)
*Zimo Ji,Zekai Zhang,Congying Xu,Zongjie Li,Yudong Gao,Shuai Wang,Shing-Chi Cheung*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出UnderSpecBench基准测试，发现未充分指定的指令导致编码Agent在DevOps任务中频繁越界（55.8%-67.8%），且目标不明确比爆炸半径更影响行为质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试侧重于任务完成，忽略了Agent在良性但未充分指定指令下的安全行为，而实际部署中错误动作可能产生严重后果。

Method: 构建UnderSpecBench，包含69个任务族，通过变化指令的意图清晰度、目标确定性和爆炸半径生成2,208个提示变体，使用确定性、基于副作用的判别器评估安全成功、错误目标和越界，并对非行为运行分类。

Result: 在五个Agent×模型配置上，55.8%-67.8%的运行违反至少一个边界；目标未充分指定性严重降低行为质量，而爆炸半径线索效果微弱。

Conclusion: 以完成为中心的评估会高估安全自主性，需要在模型、框架和系统层进行缓解，以应对未充分指定指令带来的风险。

中文摘要：LLM编码Agent被越来越多地部署在真实生产基础设施上自主行动。它们执行shell命令、修改代码仓库并调用运维API。然而，完成任务并不足以保证安全。一个错误的行为可能导致严重后果。现有的Agent基准测试主要强调任务完成，忽略了Agent在良性但未充分指定的指令下的行为。
我们提出了UnderSpecBench，一个用于衡量编码Agent（即Claude Code、Codex和OpenCode）在DevOps任务中行为边界违反的基准测试。UnderSpecBench包含69个任务族，这些任务基于已记录的事件、CVE或工具行为，并组织在四个DevOps能力领域和九个运维控制面上。为了将未充分指定性从任务难度中分离出来，每个任务保持相同的环境和真实安全行为，同时沿着三个轴变化指令：意图清晰度、目标确定性和爆炸半径。由此产生的2，208个提示变体通过确定性、基于副作用的判别器进行评估，将结果分为安全成功、错误目标和越界；非行为运行进一步分类为澄清、拒绝或延迟。
在使用OpenCode、Claude Code和Codex的五个Agent×模型配置中，评估结果表明：未充分指定性主要不是让Agent失败，而是让它们猜测。55.8%-67.8%的运行违反了至少一个边界。目标未充分指定性严重降低了行为质量，而爆炸半径线索几乎没有减少行为倾向。这些发现表明，以完成为中心的评估会高估安全自主性，并促使在模型、框架和系统层进行缓解。

Original abstract: LLM coding agents are increasingly deployed to act autonomously on real production infrastructure. They execute shell commands, modify repositories, and call operational APIs. However, completing a task is not sufficient for safety. A wrong action can cause severe consequences. Existing agent benchmarks largely emphasize task completion, leaving open how agents behave under benign but underspecified instructions.
  We present UnderSpecBench, a benchmark for measuring action-boundary violations in coding agents (i.e., Claude Code, Codex, and OpenCode) on DevOps tasks. UnderSpecBench includes 69 task families grounded in documented incidents, CVEs, or tool behavior and organized across four DevOps capability domains and nine operational control surfaces. To isolate underspecification from task difficulty, each task keeps the same environment and ground-truth safe action while varying the instruction along three axes: intent clarity, target certainty, and blast radius. The resulting 2,208 prompt variants are evaluated with deterministic, side-effect-based oracles that separate Safe Success, Wrong Target, and OverScope outcomes; non-action runs are further classified as clarification, refusal, or deferment.
  Across five agent x model configurations using OpenCode, Claude Code, and Codex, the evaluation results show that underspecification does not mainly make agents fail; it makes them guess. 55.8-67.8% of runs violate at least one boundary. Target underspecification sharply degrades action quality, while blast-radius cues barely reduce action propensity. These findings show that completion-centric evaluation can overstate safe autonomy and motivate mitigations at the model, harness, and system layer.

### [25] [Guiding Human Validation of LLM-Generated Code via Verifiable Literate Programming](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02333v1)
*Ziqi Yuan,Wenhao Lu,Hao Wu,Dunhong Jin,Chuan Wu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出VLP框架，通过无歧义的NL文档和三种技术提高LLM生成代码的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有验证方法要么依赖不可靠的LLM自动化测试，要么让用户参与有限，导致需求不明确或语义偏差等失败。

Method: VLP框架包含：无歧义NL文档作为中间层、基于LLM的细粒度不匹配检测、以及利用验证文档进行模型检查的验证模块。

Result: 在合理用户努力下，pass@1从28.7%-73.2%提升至65.4%-93.5%。

Conclusion: VLP有效提升了代码可靠性，且用户负担合理。

中文摘要：氛围编码通过允许用户通过自然语言（NL）与大语言模型（LLM）交互来生成代码，从而实现了软件开发的民主化。然而，代码只有在忠实地实现用户意图时才可靠，而用户对代码的验证既困难又劳动密集。现有的验证方法要么依赖LLM辅助的自动化测试，这存在提示歧义和模型易错性，要么仅让用户参与部分软件制品（如提示和测试用例），可能忽略边缘情况和程序细节。受LLM生成代码的错误研究启发，我们发现详细的人类反馈至关重要，因为失败通常源于未指定的需求或微妙的语义偏差。本文提出了可验证的文学编程（VLP），这是一种人机协同的框架，旨在使所有编程水平的用户都能参与到LLM生成代码的审查/验证过程中。其核心是VLP提出了无歧义的基于NL的文档，作为提示和代码之间可读的中间层。该文档展示了具体的程序语义，并允许用户提供有关意图-代码不匹配的反馈。它通过三种技术支持人工参与的端到端修复和验证：（i）一种具有无歧义语法和大部分确定性代码到文档翻译的NL风格文学语言，（ii）基于LLM的细粒度不匹配检测，利用提示和文档之间的追踪链接将用户的审查工作集中在可疑的文档行上，（iii）一个验证模块，利用用户验证过的文档导出API使用检查和形式化属性，然后通过模型检查对生成的代码进行验证。我们的评估表明，VLP在合理的用户努力下，将代码pass@1从28.7%-73.2%提高到65.4%-93.5%。

Original abstract: Vibe coding democratizes software development by allowing users to generate code via natural-language (NL) interaction with large language models (LLMs). However, the code is reliable only when it faithfully implements the user's intent, which is difficult and labor-intensive for users to validate. Existing validation methods either rely on LLM-assisted automated testing, which suffers from prompt ambiguity and model fallibility, or involve users only in partial software artifacts such as prompts and test cases, which may overlook corner cases and program details. Motivated by a bug study of LLM-generated code, we find that detailed human feedback is essential, as failures often stem from underspecified requirements or subtle semantic deviations.
  This paper presents verifiable literate programming (VLP), a human-in-the-loop framework designed to make the review/validation process of LLM-generated code accessible to users at all programming levels. At its core, VLP proposes unambiguous NL-based documentation as a readable intermediate layer between prompts and code. The documentation demonstrates concrete program semantics and enables users to provide feedback on potential intent-code mismatches. It supports human-involved, end-to-end repair and validation via three techniques: (i) an NL-style literate language with unambiguous syntax and mostly deterministic code-to-documentation translation, (ii) LLM-based fine-grained mismatch detection that uses trace links between prompts and documentation to focus users' review effort on suspicious documentation lines, and (iii) a verification module that leverages user-validated documentation to derive API-usage checks and formal properties, which are then verified against the generated code using model checking. Our evaluation shows that VLP improves code pass@1 from 28.7%-73.2% to 65.4%-93.5% with reasonable user effort.

### [26] [Developers' Experience with Generative AI Beyond Productivity Assessment -- Insights from an Empirical Mixed-Methods Field Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02337v2)
*Charlotte Brandebusemeyer,Kerim Zunic,Thomas Zimmermann,Tobias Schimmer,Bert Arnrich*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过混合方法研究发现，开发者对GenAI工具总体满意，但其交互偏好因任务类型而异；在同一任务中组合使用代码内建议和聊天提示会降低效益，而参与研究提高了开发者对工具的有意识使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究主要关注输出质量和生产力，忽视了开发者的福祉和交互体验，因此需要从开发者中心的角度进行实证研究。

Method: 以开发者为中心的实证混合方法研究，结合受控数据收集会话和自然工作时段，分析专业开发者与GenAI工具的真实互动。

Result: 开发者普遍对GenAI满意，尤其在单调重复结构化任务中；交互类型偏好因任务类型和复杂性而异，组合使用不同交互类型会降低效益；开发密集型任务中，认知负荷来自AI交互，生产力取决于输出质量；参与研究提升了开发者对工具的认识和有意使用。

Conclusion: 现实世界的混合方法研究设计对于深入理解GenAI工具及其与开发者交互的体验具有重要价值。

中文摘要：随着AI驱动的编程助手的日益普及，组织和个人开发者越来越寻求优化与这些工具的交互。先前的研究主要关注输出质量和生产力提升，而对开发者的福祉和交互体验关注有限。本文提出了一项以开发者为中心的实证混合方法研究，旨在调查专业开发者在自然工作环境中如何与生成式AI（GenAI）互动。结合了受控数据收集会话和自然工作时间。结果表明，开发者普遍对GenAI感到满意，特别是在单调、重复和结构化的任务中，并报告了感知到的效率和生产力提升。Copilot交互类型的偏好因任务类型和复杂性而异：虽然代码内建议和基于聊天的提示都能独立提高任务效率并降低感知工作负荷，但在同一任务中组合这些交互类型会削弱好处。我们提出了一条基于任务特征选择交互类型的经验法则。在开发密集型任务中，结果表明感知认知负荷源于AI交互，而感知生产力取决于AI输出质量。参与本研究积极影响了开发者对GenAI工具的认识和有意识使用。这些发现证明了现实世界混合方法研究设计在理解GenAI工具及其开发者体验方面的价值。

Original abstract: With the growing adoption of AI-powered coding assistants, organizations and developers are increasingly seeking to optimize their interaction with these tools. Prior research has largely focused on output quality and productivity gains, with limited attention paid to developers' well-being and interaction experiences. This paper presents a developer-centered empirical mixed-methods study to investigate how professional developers engage with Generative AI (GenAI) in their natural work environment. Controlled data collection sessions are combined with natural work periods. Results show that developers are generally satisfied with GenAI, particularly for monotonous, repetitive, and structured tasks, and report perceived efficiency and productivity gains. Copilot interaction type preferences differ by task type and complexity: While both in-code suggestions and chat-based prompting independently improve task efficiency and reduce perceived workload, combining these interaction types within a single task diminishes benefits. We propose a rule-of-thumb for selecting an interaction type based on task characteristics. During development-heavy tasks, results indicate that perceived cognitive load arises from AI interaction, while perceived productivity depends on AI output quality. Participation in this study positively influenced developers' awareness and intentional use of GenAI tools. These findings demonstrate the value of real-world, mixed-methods study designs to understand GenAI tools and developers' experiences with them.

### [27] [SkillFuzz: Fuzzing Skill Composition for Implicit Intents Discovery in Open Skill Marketplaces](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02345v1)
*Jinwei Hu,Yi Dong,Youcheng Sun,Xiaowei Huang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出skillfuzz方法，通过将隐式意图发现形式化为技能组合上的模糊测试问题，使用结构化技能契约和蒙特卡洛树搜索，在无需执行的情况下有效检测LLM智能体市场中良性技能组合产生的隐式意图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有市场运营商孤立审核技能，无法检测出单独良性但组合后引发非预期意图的技能交互，且执行环境缺失与组合空间爆炸使问题更具挑战。

Method: 将隐式意图发现形式化为技能组合上的模糊测试问题，提出skillfuzz方法，包括提取结构化技能契约，并采用契约引导的蒙特卡洛树搜索来优先探索可能冲突的技能组合。

Result: 在固定查询预算下发现超过1000个不同隐式意图，运行时验证中确认超过80%的高风险组合，且比替代策略发现更多高严重性意图，同时探索空间更小。

Conclusion: skillfuzz有效解决了LLM智能体市场中隐式意图的检测问题，证明了基于契约的模糊测试在技能组合空间中进行高效无执行测试的可行性。

中文摘要：基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体通过可复用技能（即指导规划与执行的自然语言指令文档）日益自动化软件工程任务。开放技能市场使得用户能够通过共同激活社区贡献的技能来组装智能体，但市场运营商通常孤立地审核技能。因此，单独良性的技能可能相互作用，将智能体引向非预期目标，我们称之为隐式意图。检测此类意图具有挑战性，因为其效果仅在技能组合中浮现，执行环境在准入时通常不可用，且可能的共激活空间随市场规模呈指数增长。本文将隐式意图发现形式化为技能组合上的模糊测试问题，其中技能组合是被测单元，计划产物在执行前暴露智能体意图，而与无技能基线的偏差则作为差异预言。基于此形式化，我们提出了skillfuzz，这是首个无需执行的测试方法，它提取结构化技能契约，并使用契约引导的蒙特卡洛树搜索来优先处理潜在冲突的组合。在代表性技能市场工作负载上，skillfuzz在固定查询预算下发现了超过1000个不同的隐式意图，在运行时验证中确认了超过80%的最高风险被标记组合，并且与替代搜索策略相比，识别出更多高严重性的隐式意图，同时仅探索了它们所需的成对交互空间的一小部分。

Original abstract: Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents increasingly automate software engineering tasks through reusable skills, natural-language instruction documents that guide planning and execution. Open skill marketplaces enable users to assemble agents by co-activating community-contributed skills, but marketplace operators typically audit skills in isolation. As a result, individually benign skills may interact to redirect an agent toward unintended objectives, which we term implicit intents. Detecting such intents is challenging because the effect emerges only through skill composition, execution environments are often unavailable at admission time, and the space of possible co-activations grows exponentially with marketplace size. In this paper, we formulate implicit-intent discovery as a fuzzing problem over skill compositions, where skill compositions are the unit under test, planning artifacts expose agent intent before execution, and deviations from a skill-free baseline serve as a differential oracle. Based on this formulation, we propose skillfuzz, the first execution-free testing approach that extracts structured skill contracts and uses contract-guided Monte Carlo Tree Search to prioritize potentially conflicting compositions. Across representative skill-marketplace workloads, skillfuzz discovers over 1,000 distinct implicit intents under a fixed query budget, confirms more than 80% of the highest-risk flagged compositions during execution-time validation, and identifies substantially more high-severity implicit intents than alternative search strategies while exploring only a fraction of the pairwise interaction space they require.

</details>


### [28] [Understanding Agent-Based Patching of Compiler Missed Optimizations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02370v2)
*Batu Guan,Zirui Wang,Shaohua Li*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了代理修补编译器错过优化的能力，发现代理生成的补丁在优化范围上与开发者补丁存在差异，并提出了历史知识增强技术以改善泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 编译器错过优化需要大量开发人员修补，而代理修补面临泛化挑战，即不仅修复具体案例，还需推广到类似情况。

Method: 构建了真实世界LLVM错过优化问题的基准，比较代理与开发者补丁的优化范围，并引入基于检索和蒸馏的历史知识增强技术。

Result: 代理常优化给定示例，但补丁多只部分覆盖开发者意图范围，甚至过度泛化；历史知识增强技术提升了与开发者对齐的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 历史知识增强技术在真实世界IR中带来实际效益，有助于代理生成更符合开发者意图的补丁。

中文摘要：编译器错过的优化是指编译器未能优化某些代码的情况。实现或修补这些错过的优化需要许多编译器开发人员的努力。在本文中，我们系统性地研究了代理(agent)修补编译器错过的优化的能力。我们识别了一个重大挑战：修补错过的优化不仅仅需要修复报告的具体案例，还需要泛化到类似案例。我们构建了一个真实世界LLVM错过优化问题的基准，并从优化范围的角度比较了代理生成的补丁与开发人员生成的补丁。我们的结果表明，编码代理经常优化给定的示例，但许多生成的补丁要么只覆盖了开发人员预期范围的一部分，要么与之部分重叠；在某些情况下，它们甚至进一步泛化到参考补丁之外。我们进一步引入了历史知识增强技术，通过检索和蒸馏利用先前的LLVM优化拉取请求，表明这些技术改善了与开发人员对齐的泛化，并在应用于真实世界IR时产生了实际效益。

Original abstract: Compiler missed optimizations refer to cases in which compilers failed to optimize certain code. It takes many compiler developers' efforts to implement or patch such missed optimizations. In this paper, we present a systematic study of how well agents patch compiler missed optimizations. We identify a significant challenge that patching a missed optimization requires more than just fixing the reported case, and instead requires generalizing to similar cases. We construct a benchmark of real-world LLVM missed optimization issues and compare agent-generated patches with patches from developers in terms of optimization scope. Our results show that coding agents often optimize the given examples, but many generated patches either cover only part of the developer-intended scope or partially overlap with it; in some cases, they further generalize beyond the reference patch. We further introduce historical-knowledge augmentation techniques that leverage prior LLVM optimization pull requests through retrieval and distillation, showing that they improve developer-aligned generalization and yield practical benefits when applied to real-world IR.
