### [29] [Reasoning effort, not tool access, buys first-try reliability in agentic code generation: an observational study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02436v1)
*Achint Mehta*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过90次独立智能体运行构建同一应用，发现能力层级（尤其是推理能力）比附加工具对软件质量影响更大，测试工具增加成本但无益，提高推理努力显著改善性能，设计提示提升视觉质量但不影响功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前智能编码助手被赋予更多能力（如测试工具、设计提示）基于“更多能力更好软件”的假设，但该假设未经直接检验。

Method: 使用90次独立智能体运行构建同一实时回顾板应用，通过14项功能评分（满分42）和视觉质量评分，比较不同模型世代、智能体框架、推理努力水平、测试工具和设计提示的影响。

Result: 前沿模型得分接近满分，低成本模型得分低；容器部署失败率高；测试工具增加成本但不改善功能或可靠性；提高推理努力显著提升首次完美率并减少纠正提示；设计提示提升视觉质量但不改善功能。

Conclusion: 应根据失败原因选择修复：多数首次运行失败源于弱推理而非可见缺陷，应优先提升推理能力而非添加检查工具。

中文摘要：智能编码助手被越来越多地赋予额外能力，例如基于浏览器的测试工具和面向设计的系统提示，其假设是更多能力会带来更好的软件。本研究直接检验了这一假设。90次独立的智能体运行从一份详细规格说明构建了同一个应用程序（一个实时回顾板），每次运行根据固定的14项标准功能评分表（满分42分）和视觉质量评审进行评分。这些运行跨越了多个模型世代、两个智能体框架、两种推理努力水平、一个测试工具和两种面向设计的提示。能力层级起主导作用：前沿模型集中在接近满分的位置，而低成本本地模型得分在24到37分之间。一项标准层面的分析揭示了运行总分所掩盖的内容。容器部署是主要缺陷，44%的运行首次尝试失败，其失败率在不同模型世代间急剧变化，而平均总分的变化不到一分。测试工具使成本增加了42%到68%，但没有改善功能得分或可靠性，即使是对界面可见的标准也是如此。将推理努力从高提高到极高，使得首次尝试完美的运行从28%提高到89%，并将纠正提示减少了大约五倍，而成本增加了9%到29%。面向设计的提示提高了视觉质量（5分制中4.5分对3.0分），但没有提升功能，并且其指令的一段 paraphrase 完全复制了这种提升。实际教训是让修复匹配失败：大多数首次运行失败来自弱推理，这可以通过更强的模型或更多的努力来预防，而不是通过检查工具能捕捉到的可见缺陷。

Original abstract: Agentic coding assistants are increasingly given extra capabilities, such as browser based testing tools and design oriented system prompts, on the assumption that more capability yields better software. This study tested that assumption directly. Ninety independent agent runs built the same application, a real time retrospective board, from one detailed specification, each scored on a fixed 14 criterion functional rubric (42 point maximum) and a visual quality review. The runs spanned several model generations, two agent harnesses, two reasoning effort levels, a testing tool, and two design oriented prompts. Capability tier dominated: frontier models clustered near the ceiling while a low cost local model fell to 24 to 37 points. A criterion level analysis revealed what run totals conceal. Container deployment was the dominant defect, failing first try in 44 percent of runs, with its failure rate shifting sharply across model generations while mean totals moved less than a point. The testing tool raised cost by 42 to 68 percent without improving functional score or reliability, even on interface visible criteria. Raising reasoning effort from High to xHigh lifted first try perfect runs from 28 percent to 89 percent and cut corrective prompts about five fold, for 9 to 29 percent more cost. A design oriented prompt raised visual quality, 4.5 versus 3.0 on a 5 point scale, without lifting function, and a one paragraph paraphrase of its directive reproduced the entire lift. The practical lesson is to match the fix to the failure: most first run failures came from weak reasoning, which a stronger model or more effort prevents, not from visible flaws a checking tool would catch.

</details>


### [30] [HTTP REST API Structure Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02442v1)
*Ran Dubin,Amit Dvir*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: HRAL是一种无监督异常检测方法，直接从网络流量学习API行为，在文档有限时仍能高效检测恶意活动，结合签名规则达100%检测率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: API广泛使用带来安全风险，现有方法依赖规则或文档，但在实际中API文档往往不完整，需要一种不依赖预定义规则的异常检测方法。

Method: 提出HRAL，一种无监督异常检测方法，直接从网络流量中学习API端点的结构和行为，通过建模行为并标记偏离为威胁。

Result: 平均召回82.07%，F1分数87.24%，优于现有方法；结合OWASP ModSecurity CRS规则时检测率达100%。

Conclusion: HRAL在部分文档化的API环境下有效，可作为现代API安全解决方案的基础层，提升检测能力。

中文摘要：应用程序编程接口（API）在软件开发中至关重要，支持网络服务、移动应用和微服务。然而，它们的广泛使用引入了显著的安全风险，凸显了API安全的重要性。本文提出了HTTP REST API学习（HRAL），一种新颖的无监督异常检测方法，直接从网络流量中建模API端点的结构和行为，无需依赖预定义规则或文档。HRAL通过理解API的行为并将偏差标记为潜在威胁，实现对恶意活动的强大检测。我们在不同OpenAPI文档详细程度下评估HRAL，并将其与现有技术进行比较。HRAL表现出强劲性能，平均召回率为82.07%，F1分数为87.24%，在API文档有限时显著优于替代方案。此外，我们的结果接近完整API文档定义的有效性。当与基于签名的规则（如OWASP ModSecurity CRS）结合时，我们的系统实现了100%的检测率。这些结果突显了HRAL在现实世界中部分文档化的API环境中的有效性，以及其作为现代API安全解决方案基础层的潜力。

Original abstract: Application Programming Interfaces (APIs) are essential in software development, enabling web services, mobile apps, and microservices. However, their widespread use introduces significant security risks, highlighting the importance of API security. This paper presents HTTP REST API Learning (HRAL), a novel unsupervised anomaly detection approach that models the structure and behavior of API endpoints directly from network traffic, without relying on predefined rules or documentation. HRAL enables robust detection of malicious activity by understanding how APIs behave and flagging deviations as potential threats. We evaluate HRAL across varying levels of OpenAPI documentation detail and compare it with existing techniques. HRAL achieves strong performance, with an average recall of 82.07% and an F1-score of 87.24%, significantly outperforming alternatives when API documentation is limited. Moreover, our results approach the effectiveness of full API document definitions. When combined with signature-based rules such as the OWASP ModSecurity CRS, our system achieves 100% detection. These results highlight HRAL's effectiveness in real-world, partially documented API environments and its potential as a foundational layer for modern API security solutions.

### [31] [TestEvo-Bench: An Executable and Live Benchmark for Test and Code Co-Evolution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02469v1)
*Jiale Amber Wang,Kaiyuan Wang,Pengyu Nie*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: TestEvo-Bench是一个测试与代码共同演化基准，基于真实提交历史，提供执行指标和实时更新以减少数据泄露。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准将测试与代码变更隔离，依赖静态元数据，无法验证测试的可执行性和语义关联，难以评估代理对变更传播的理解。

Method: 从152个Java项目的59,950个候选记录中挖掘出746个测试生成和509个测试更新任务，每个任务包含环境配置以计算通过率、覆盖率和变异得分，并基于时间戳定期更新。

Result: 四种先进代理在测试生成上最高77.5%成功率，测试更新上74.6%，但最新任务和有限成本下成功率显著下降。

Conclusion: TestEvo-Bench有效评估测试自动化代理，但最新任务和成本限制仍是挑战。

中文摘要：软件测试和代码共同演化：代码更改后应随后进行新的或更新的测试，以记录新的软件行为。然而，现有的测试生成和更新基准常常将测试与代码变更隔离开，并依赖静态元数据，这些元数据不验证测试是否可执行或与代码变更在语义上关联。这使得难以评估测试自动化代理是否理解代码变更应如何传播到测试套件中。我们引入了TestEvo-Bench，这是一个从软件仓库中挖掘出的测试与代码共同演化任务的基准，包含两个方向：在测试生成中，代理应编写新的测试以捕获新的软件行为；在测试更新中，代理应调整现有的失败测试以适应变更后的软件行为。每个任务都锚定到一个真实的提交历史，并附带环境配置以支持基于执行的指标，如通过率、覆盖率和变异得分。TestEvo-Bench也是一个实时基准：每个任务记录测试和代码变更的时间戳，新任务由我们的自动化流水线定期挖掘，因此评估可以限制在模型训练截止日期之后的任务，以减少数据泄露风险。当前快照包含746个测试生成和509个测试更新任务，这些任务来自152个开源Java项目的59,950个候选共同演化记录。我们实验了四种最先进的代理，它们结合了强大的工具（Claude Code, Gemini CLI, 和 SWE-Agent）与强大的基础模型（Claude Opus 4.7 和 Gemini 3.1 Pro）。结果表明，它们在测试生成上取得了高达77.5%的成功率，在测试更新上达到了74.6%。然而，在最新的基准任务上成功率明显较低，并且在有限的每任务成本下显著下降。

Original abstract: Software tests and code evolve together: a code change should be followed by new or updated tests that record the new software behavior. Yet existing test generation and update benchmarks often isolate the test from the code change, and rely on static metadata that does not verify whether a test is executable or semantically tied to the code change. This makes it difficult to evaluate whether a test automation agent understands how a code change should propagate into the test suite.
  We introduce TestEvo-Bench, a benchmark of test and code co-evolution tasks mined from software repositories, with two tracks: in test generation, the agent shall write new tests to capture the new software behavior; in test update, the agent shall adapt failing existing tests to the changed software behavior. Each task is anchored to a real commit history and packaged with environment configuration to support execution-grounded metrics such as pass rate, coverage, and mutation score. TestEvo-Bench is also a live benchmark: each task records the timestamp of the test and code changes, and new tasks are periodically mined by our automated pipeline, so evaluation can be restricted to tasks postdating a model's training cutoff to reduce data leakage risk. The current snapshot contains 746 test generation and 509 test update tasks, curated from 59,950 candidate co-evolution records across 152 open-source Java projects. We experiment with four state-of-the-art agents that combine strong harnesses (Claude Code, Gemini CLI, and SWE-Agent) with strong foundation models (Claude Opus 4.7 and Gemini 3.1 Pro). Results show that they achieve up to 77.5% success rate on test generation and 74.6% on test update. However, success rate is materially lower on the most recent benchmark tasks and drops significantly under limited per-task cost.

</details>


### [32] [Can Coding Agents Implement Missed Compiler Optimizations? Evaluating LLM Agents on LLVM Peephole Optimizations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02684v1)
*Hongxu Xu,Chunhao Liao,Xintong Zhou,Chengnian Sun*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: PeepholeBench是一个评估编码智能体修复LLVM编译器遗漏窥孔优化的基准，发现当前智能体在正确性和收益性上均无法匹敌人类开发者，主要失败模式为转换过窄和LLVM机制误用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有编码智能体在代码补丁方面表现出色，但能否开发编译器优化（尤其是需要语义推理和优化器知识的窥孔优化）尚不清楚，缺乏系统评估基准。

Method: 构建PeepholeBench任务：从21个已解决LLVM问题和19个合并PR中提取真实窥孔优化案例，仅提供修复前的issue上下文，评估智能体生成的补丁的正确性和收益性，并与人类修复对比。

Result: 无智能体能在正确性和收益性上同时匹敌人类；主要失败模式包括过于狭窄的转换和LLVM特定机制误用（如模式匹配错误），这些错误难以被现有测试套件捕获。

Conclusion: PeepholeBench是一个逼真且富有挑战性的基准，揭示了当前编码智能体在编译器优化任务中的局限性，未来需构建能更可靠推理程序语义并避免特定机制误用的智能体。

中文摘要：基于大型语言模型的编码智能体现在能够修补可观的真实世界代码库，但它们能否开发编译器优化仍然是一个开放问题。为了研究这一问题，我们引入了PeepholeBench，这是一个评估框架，其任务来源于针对LLVM的InstCombine pass报告的真实世界遗漏窥孔优化。由于遗漏的窥孔优化通常通过小而局部的补丁修复，它们为编码智能体提供了一个范围明确但要求严格的测试平台：正确的修复需要对程序语义进行严谨推理，并熟悉优化器特定的约定。PeepholeBench的任务源自21个已解决的LLVM问题和19个合并的拉取请求（PR），仅向智能体提供每个修复之前存在的issue上下文，并评估生成的补丁的正确性和收益性。通过PeepholeBench，我们评估了最先进的编码智能体修复LLVM InstCombine pass中遗漏窥孔优化的能力，并将其补丁与对应的人工编写的修复进行比较。我们观察到正确性与收益性之间存在张力，没有智能体能在两个维度上同时匹敌人类开发者。主要的失败模式是过于狭窄的转换以及对LLVM特定机制的误用，这些错误现有的测试套件很少能暴露。这些结果共同确立了PeepholeBench作为编码智能体的一个真实且具有挑战性的基准，并为构建能够更可靠地协助编译器优化开发的智能体指明了未来方向。

Original abstract: Coding agents built on large language models are now capable of patching sizable real-world codebases, yet whether they can develop compiler optimizations remains an open question. To study this question, we introduce PeepholeBench, an evaluation framework whose tasks are constructed from real-world missed peephole optimizations reported against LLVM's InstCombine pass. Since missed peephole optimizations are typically fixed with small, localized patches, they offer a well-scoped but demanding testbed for coding agents: a correct fix demands rigorous reasoning about program semantics along with familiarity with optimizer-specific conventions. PeepholeBench derives its tasks from 21 resolved LLVM issues and 19 merged pull requests (PRs), supplies agents with only the issue context that existed before each fix, and assesses the resulting patches for both correctness and profitability.
  With PeepholeBench, we benchmark state-of-the-art coding agents on fixing missed peephole optimizations in LLVM's InstCombine pass, measuring their patches against the corresponding human-written fixes. We observe a tension between correctness and profitability, and no agent matches human developers on both dimensions at once. The dominant failure modes are overly narrow transformations and misuse of LLVM-specific mechanisms, errors that existing test suites rarely expose. Together, these results establish PeepholeBench as a realistic and challenging benchmark for coding agents, and suggest future directions for building agents that can more dependably assist compiler optimization development.

### [33] [LLMoxie: Exploring Agentic AI for Scientific Software Development](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02703v1)
*Landung Setiawan,Anant Mittal,Cordero Core,Anshul Tambay,Carlos Garcia Jurado Suarez,David A. C. Beck,Andrew J. Connolly,Vani Mandava*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文介绍LLMoxie平台及其RSE插件生态，通过三层架构和知识编码，使AI编码代理适应科研软件需求，实现领域感知和可审计协作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现成AI编码代理忽视科学Python库约定、误处理敏感数据、决策轨迹难追踪，无法满足科学软件对可引用、审计、复现和扩展的要求。

Method: 设计LLMoxie平台（三层架构：多云/本地推理层、LiteLLM/MLflow控制平面、应用增强层）及开源RSE-Plugins生态（插件-代理-技能层次），并在多领域RSE中心进行二十个月实践。

Result: 识别出基础设施、治理和流程挑战，从真实部署中提炼运营经验，使AI代理成为领域感知、遵守社区规范且提供可审计推理溯源的协作者。

Conclusion: 平台和插件有效将AI编码代理从通用代码生成器转变为适合科学软件的领域感知协作工具，提升代码可审计性和可复现性。

中文摘要：在本文中，我们描述了LLMoxie，一个机构级AI平台，其三层架构支持多云和本地推理，一个用于认证、预算、PII屏蔽和可观测性的LiteLLM/MLflow控制平面，以及用于AI编码代理的应用增强层。在此基础上，一个开源的RSE-Plugins生态系统将积累的RSE知识编码为插件-代理-技能层次结构，涵盖科学Python实践、领域特定知识、六阶段研究与实现工作流以及项目生命周期管理。科学软件的评价较少依据原始代码质量，而更多取决于其是否可被引用、审计、复现和扩展。针对商业软件基准优化的现成AI编码代理在这种情况下校准不良：它们忽略所调用的科学Python库的约定，误处理敏感或受限数据，并留下事后难以重建的决策轨迹。我们报告了在一个大学研究软件工程（RSE）中心二十个月的实践，该中心嵌入天文学、地球与气候科学、农业和健康项目的RSE致力于缩小这一差距。我们描述了在多领域RSE中心采用代理式AI时反复出现的基础设施、治理和流程挑战，介绍了平台和插件设计，并从实际科学软件部署中提炼出运营经验。平台和插件共同将AI编码代理从通用代码生成器转变为尊重社区规范并产生可审计技术推理溯源的领域感知协作者。

Original abstract: In this paper, we describe LLMoxie, an institutional AI platform whose three-tiered architecture supports multi-cloud and on-premise inference, a LiteLLM/MLflow control plane for authentication, budgeting, PII masking, and observability, and an application augmentation layer for AI coding agents. Layered on top, an open-source RSE-Plugins ecosystem encodes accumulated RSE knowledge as a Plugin-Agent-Skill hierarchy spanning scientific Python practice, domain-specific knowledge, a six-phase research-and-implement workflow, and project lifecycle management. Scientific software is judged less by raw code quality than by whether it can be cited, audited, reproduced, and extended. Off-the-shelf AI coding agents, optimized against commercial software benchmarks, are poorly calibrated for this setting: they ignore the conventions of the scientific Python libraries they invoke, mishandle sensitive or embargoed data, and leave decision trails that are difficult to reconstruct after the fact. We report on twenty months of practice at a university-based research software engineering (RSE) center, where RSEs embedded across astronomy, earth and climate science, agriculture, and health projects worked to close this gap. We characterize the recurring infrastructure, governance, and process challenges of adopting Agentic AI inside a multi-domain RSE center, describe the platform and plugin design, and distill operational lessons from real scientific software deployments. Together, the platform and plugins shift AI coding agents from generic code generators into domain-aware collaborators that respect community norms and produce auditable provenance of technical reasoning.

### [34] [SMOCS: A Streaming Framework for Simplified Deployment, Monitoring, and Optimization of ML Systems in Production](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02731v1)
*Armen Kasparian,Kishansingh Rajput,Malachi Schram,John Vennekate*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: SMOCS是一个基于Kafka的容器化框架，通过分层抽象、三线程代理架构和配置驱动部署，解决了科学设施中ML模型部署的工程挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学设施中ML模型的部署和维护面临巨大工程挑战，主要是每个设施独特的数据协议和基础设施限制导致需要重复构建集成管道。

Method: 提出SMOCS框架，包括：1）对Kafka的分层抽象实现基础设施与应用逻辑分离；2）三线程代理架构实现数据摄入、模型训练和实时推理的时间解耦；3）配置驱动部署模型使领域专家无需软件工程知识即可操作ML管道。

Result: SMOCS实现设施平台无关、故障隔离、水平可扩展，并作为开源软件在Jefferson Lab GitHub发布。

Conclusion: SMOCS有效降低了ML部署的工程复杂度，使领域专家能直接操作ML管道，为科学设施的实时监控、优化和控制提供了可扩展的解决方案。

中文摘要：机器学习已展现出在科学设施的实时监控、优化和控制方面的巨大潜力。然而，在运行环境中部署和维护机器学习模型仍然是一项重大的工程挑战。每个设施都有独特的数据协议、非标准格式和基础设施限制，迫使团队为每个新应用重建集成管道。我们提出SMOCS（流式监控优化与控制系统），这是一个基于Kafka的容器化框架，通过三个贡献来解决这一挑战：1）对Apache Kafka的分层抽象，将基础设施与应用逻辑分离；2）三线程代理架构，在时间上解耦数据摄入、模型训练和实时推理，实现对实时数据流的持续在线学习；3）配置驱动的部署模型，使领域专家能够在没有软件工程专业知识的情况下操作机器学习管道。SMOCS与设施平台无关，设计上具有故障隔离，并通过Docker容器化实现水平可扩展。该框架作为开源软件在Jefferson Lab的GitHub上公开发布。

Original abstract: Machine learning has demonstrated significant potential for real-time monitoring, optimization, and control of scientific facilities. However, deploying and maintaining ML models in operational environments remains a substantial engineering challenge. Each facility presents unique data protocols, non-standard formats, and infrastructure constraints, forcing teams to rebuild integration pipelines for every new application. We present SMOCS (Streaming Monitoring Optimization and Control System), a Kafka-based containerized framework that addresses this challenge through three contributions: 1) a layered abstraction over Apache Kafka that separates infrastructure from application logic, 2) a three-thread agent architecture that temporally decouples data ingestion, model training, and real-time inference enabling continuous online learning from live data streams, and 3) a configuration-driven deployment model that enables domain experts to operate ML pipelines without software engineering expertise. SMOCS is facility platform-agnostic, fault-isolated by design, and horizontally scalable through Docker containerization. The framework is publicly available as open-source software on the Jefferson Lab Github.

### [35] [Benefits of Applying Software Design Patterns to Backend Rust Applications](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02744v1)
*Leon Heuer*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过案例研究评估Rust中typestate和newtype模式对代码质量的影响，发现typestate提升无故障性但增加代码结构，newtype结合“解析，不要验证”以低成本提高质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Rust语言具有新颖的语言特性，但设计模式对其代码质量影响的研究很少，需要实证评估。

Method: 对三个生产后端组件进行案例研究，基于SQuaRE质量模型构建评估框架，应用typestate和newtype模式重构，并通过基准测试、静态分析和专家访谈评估。

Result: Typestate模式显著提高无故障性和可测试性，但增加结构代码可能降低可读性；newtype模式结合“解析，不要验证”原则以低成本提高质量并防止运行时无效状态。

Conclusion: 提供了Rust设计模式的初步实证评估，为未来更多用例和模式的研究奠定了基础。

中文摘要：关于软件设计模式对代码质量的影响，大部分研究都是在面向对象语言的背景下进行的。而在编程语言Rust中，它拥有新颖的语言概念、编译时安全保证和独特的类型系统，关于设计模式的研究却很少。本研究通过一个针对生产后端应用程序的三个代表性组件的案例研究，调查了模式如何影响软件质量和不变量的编译时强制执行。我们开发了一个基于SQuaRE质量模型标准的评估框架，结合基准测试、静态代码分析和专家访谈，来评估重构后的代码。应用了typestate和newtype模式来解决选定用例中现有的代码异味。虽然typestate模式显著提高了无故障性和可测试性，但代价是增加了结构代码，可能降低可读性。具有大量分支逻辑和许多不变量的代码可能从该模式中受益最多。结合“解析，不要验证”原则的newtype模式以低成本提供了软件质量的高回报，并防止了运行时无效状态。总体而言，这项工作为Rust中的设计模式提供了初步的实证评估，并为涉及更多用例和模式的进一步研究奠定了基础。

Original abstract: Software design patterns' effects on code quality have mostly been studied in the context of object-oriented languages. In the programming language Rust, which comes with novel language concepts, compile-time safety guarantees and a distinct type system, there has been little research on design patterns. This work investigates how patterns affect software quality and compile-time enforcement of invariants through a case study on three representative components of production backend applications. An evaluation framework based on criteria derived from the SQuaRE quality model, incorporating benchmarking, static code analysis and expert interviews, is developed to assess the refactored code. The patterns typestate and newtype are applied to address existing code smells in the selected use cases. While the typestate pattern improves faultlessness and testability significantly, it comes at the cost of more structural code that can degrade readability. Code with extensive branching logic and a high number of invariants is likely to benefit most from the pattern. The newtype pattern combined with the "Parse, don't validate" principle offers high returns in software quality at a low cost and prevents invalid states during runtime. Overall, this work provides an initial empirical assessment of design patterns in Rust and establishes a foundation for further studies involving additional use cases and patterns.

</details>


### [36] [From Codebases to LLMs: Non-Inclusive Naming in Linux Foundation Repositories](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02772v2)
*Honghao Tan,Md Nafiu Rahman,Shin Hwei Tan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 首个关于Linux基金会项目中包容性命名采纳的生态系统规模研究，发现非包容性术语减少47%但仍有62.7%仓库存在残留，且LLMs能从上下文重构旧标识符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺乏对LF项目中包容性命名长期采纳及对AI开发影响的实证证据。

Method: 开发NISCAN静态分析框架，对461个LF仓库进行分析，并进行LLM案例研究。

Result: 非包容性术语减少47%，62.7%仓库仍有残留；术语残留主要在文档等；项目特征比治理更能预测包容性；LLMs能从上下文重构旧标识符。

Conclusion: 首个生态规模评估，强调处理术语残留对负责任命名和代码生成的重要性。

中文摘要：自2020年以来，Linux基金会和多个组织组成的包容性命名倡议（INI）鼓励开源项目替换如master/slave和whitelist/blacklist等非包容性术语。尽管这些建议已被广泛采纳，但关于它们在Linux基金会（LF）项目中的长期采纳情况以及对AI辅助软件开发的影响，仍缺乏实证证据。在本文中，我们提出了NISCAN，一个多语言静态分析框架，使用INI词汇表检测源代码及相关软件制品中的非包容性术语。利用NISCAN，我们首次对461个Linux基金会仓库进行了生态系统规模上的包容性命名研究。我们的分析显示，自2020年以来，非包容性术语减少了约47%，但采纳仍不完全：62.7%的仓库仍包含至少一个一级非包容性标识符，而剩余术语大多位于源代码之外的文档、注释、配置文件和其他软件制品中。我们进一步表明，仓库规模、编程语言、项目功能和生态系统是LF仓库中术语包容性的更强预测因素，而非基金会治理。为了研究对AI辅助软件开发的启示，我们进行了一个案例研究，评估大型语言模型（LLMs）能否从周围的程序上下文中重构遗留的非包容性标识符。结果显示，即使在标识符被重命名后，历史命名决策仍然嵌入在模型预测中。总体而言，我们的研究结果提供了Linux基金会内包容性命名采纳的首个生态系统规模评估，并强调了处理术语残留对于支持负责任的命名和合乎道德的代码生成的重要性。

Original abstract: Since 2020, the Linux Foundation and the multi-organization Inclusive Naming Initiative (INI) have encouraged open-source projects to replace non-inclusive terms such as master/slave and whitelist/blacklist. Although these recommendations have been widely adopted, there is limited empirical evidence on their long-term adoption across Linux Foundation (LF) projects or their implications for AI-assisted software development. In this paper, we present NISCAN, a multilingual static-analysis framework that detects non-inclusive terminology across source code and related software artifacts using the INI vocabulary. Using NISCAN, we conduct the first ecosystem-scale study of inclusive naming across 461 Linux Foundation repositories. Our analysis shows that non-inclusive terminology has declined by approximately 47% since 2020, yet adoption remains incomplete: 62.7% of repositories still contain at least one Tier-1 non-inclusive identifier, while most remaining terminology resides outside source code in documentation, comments, configuration files, and other software artifacts. We further show that repository size, programming language, project functionality, and ecosystem are stronger predictors of term inclusiveness in LF repositories rather than foundation governance. To examine the implications for AI-assisted software development, we conduct a case study evaluating whether large language models (LLMs) can reconstruct legacy non-inclusive identifiers from surrounding program context. The results show that historical naming decisions remain embedded in model predictions even after identifiers have been renamed. Overall, our study findings provide the first ecosystem-scale assessment of inclusive naming adoption within the Linux Foundation and highlight the importance of addressing terminology residue to support responsible naming and ethically sourced code generation.

### [37] [Was It Never Collected, or Rewritten Away? A Commit-Provenance Dataset Separating Ingestion Gaps from Upstream History Edits across the World of Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02774v1)
*Audris Mockus*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过对比GHArchive事件流和WoC对象数据库，区分了镜像中缺失提交的两种原因（强制推送重写 vs 从未采集），并发布了大规模数据集以量化各类别的比例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决开源版本控制全局镜像不完整的问题，准确区分强制推送导致的提交消失与镜像真实采集缺口，提高镜像完整性报告的可靠性。

Method: 比较GHArchive事件流（推送时广告的提交）和WoC V2604对象数据库（已采集的提交），通过重构PushEvent链检测强制推送（断开的快进链），并联合WoC成员身份对每个广告提交标记为“存在”、“重写”或“从未摄取”。

Result: 在11亿广告提交中，53.35%存在，6.47%被重写，40.18%从未摄取；发布强制推送事件和项目级汇总；指出40%是采集缺口上限并给出高估原因；历史编辑导致提交计数低估10.82%。

Conclusion: 该数据集提升镜像完整性评估的准确性，可识别因强制推送而丢失的提交（占缺失案例的1/15），纠正基于提交的生产力统计中的低估，并提供修正因子。

中文摘要：任何开源版本控制的全局镜像都是不完整的，但提交缺失的原因不可互换：项目可能强制推送将其移除（因此上游不再存在），或者镜像可能从未摄取过它（真正的收集缺口）。我们发布了一个提交来源数据集，通过比较同一提交图的两种视图来大规模区分这些情况：GHArchive事件流（推送时GitHub广告内容的历史见证）和世界代码（WoC）V2604对象数据库（定期抓取的累积联合，从不删除已收集的提交）。遍历每个引用的PushEvent链从结构上重构强制推送（之前不是先前的头会破坏快进链；跨时代没有记录标志），并将每个广告的提交与WoC成员身份进行连接，产生三路标签。在1,118,116,350个广告提交中，53.35%存在于WoC中，6.47%被重写（因后续强制推送、上游编辑和正确缺失而成为孤儿），40.18%从未被摄取（候选收集缺口）。大约十五个缺失提交案例中有一个是项目擦除的重写，而不是镜像缺口。我们发布了强制推送见证（19,926,250个仓库上的166,710,831个事件）和每个项目的汇总（78,125,788个仓库；在25.47%中观察到强制推送，在12.85%中观察到重写提交）。我们将40%的从未摄取份额视为收集缺口的上限，并陈述了五个高估原因。该数据集使镜像完整性报告诚实，将重写提交标记为贡献计数的重复补丁来源，并纠正了历史编辑对基于提交的生产力施加的10.82%的全语料低估，同时发布了每个项目的修正因子。所有制品作为一个独立托管的、与WoC V2604关联的自包含复制包提供。

Original abstract: Any global mirror of open-source version control is incomplete, but the reasons a commit is missing are not interchangeable: a project may have force-pushed it away (so it no longer exists upstream), or the mirror may never have ingested it (a true collection gap). We release a commit-provenance dataset that separates these cases at scale by comparing two views of the same commit graph: the GHArchive event stream, a historical witness of what GitHub advertised at push time, and the World of Code (WoC) V2604 object database, an accumulated union of periodic fetches that never deletes a collected commit. Walking each reference's PushEvent chain reconstructs force-pushes structurally (a before that is not the prior head breaks the fast-forward chain; no recorded flag exists across eras), and joining every advertised commit against WoC membership yields a three-way label. Over 1,118,116,350 advertised commits, 53.35% are present in WoC, 6.47% are rewritten (orphaned by a later force-push, an upstream edit and a correct absence), and 40.18% are never-ingested (the candidate collection gap). About one missing-commit case in fifteen is a rewrite the project erased, not a mirror gap. We release the force-push witness (166,710,831 events over 19,926,250 repositories) and a per-project rollup (78,125,788 repositories; force-pushing observed in 25.47%, a rewritten commit in 12.85%). We treat the 40% never-ingested share as an upper bound on the collection gap and state five reasons it overcounts. The dataset makes mirror-completeness reporting honest, flags rewritten commits as duplicate patch sources for contribution counting, and corrects a 10.82% corpus-wide undercount that history editing imposes on commit-based productivity, with a released per-project correction factor. All artifacts ship as a self-contained, independently hosted replication package keyed to WoC V2604.

</details>


### [38] [A Preliminary Study on Explaining Risk of Code Changes using LLM-Based Prediction Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02782v1)
*Yalin Liu,Kosay Jabre,Rui Abreu,Zachariah J. Carmichael,Vijayaraghavan Murali,Akshay Patel,Jun Ge,Weiyan Sun,Cong Zhang,Audris Mockus,David Khavari,Peter C. Rigby,Nachiappan Nagappan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 利用LLM注意力权重突出显示代码变更中的风险部分，在覆盖53.85%专家标注的故障行时只需审查26.28%的变更行，且可扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习预测常因缺乏可解释性而遭质疑，现有研究较少关注在即时缺陷预测中利用注意力机制突出显示代码变更（diff）中的风险集中区域，以提供轻量级指导。

Method: 使用基于LLM的Diff Risk Score (DRS)模型的注意力权重，将token级注意力聚合成行、块、文件等可解释单元，选择前K个单元向开发者展示。

Result: 在专家标注的故障数据集上，突出显示前2个块时覆盖了53.85%的故障行，开发者只需审查平均26.28%的变更行。

Conclusion: 该方法利用模型推理过程中产生的注意力，无需额外开销，可扩展至大型开发流程，并能集成到代码审查UI中提供实时指导。

中文摘要：机器学习（ML）和人工智能（AI）模型的预测常常受到质疑，除非配以可理解的解释。在即时缺陷预测的背景下，突出显示软件变更（diff）中风险可能集中的小部分（超越基于规则的检查）尚未得到广泛研究。在这项工作中，我们利用基于LLM的差异风险评分（DRS）模型的注意力权重，突出显示模型在预测风险时关注的diff部分。我们将token级别的注意力聚合成可解释的代码单元（行、块和文件），并将前K个单元呈现给开发者，作为代码审查期间的一种轻量级指导。我们使用导致实际宕机的专家标注变更来评估我们的方法。结果表明，在突出显示前2个块时，突出显示的片段覆盖了专家标注的导致宕机的变更行，覆盖率为53.85%，同时要求开发者平均审查26.28%的变更行。由于注意力是在标准模型推理过程中产生的，该方法可扩展到大型开发工作流，并且可以以较低额外延迟在代码审查UI中呈现。

Original abstract: Predictions by machine learning (ML) and artificial intelligence (AI) models are often received skeptically unless they are paired with intelligible explanations. In the context of just-in-time defect prediction, highlighting small portions of a software change (diff) -- beyond rule-based lints -- where risk may be concentrated has not yet been extensively investigated. In this work, we leverage attention weights from an LLM-based Diff Risk Score (DRS) model to highlight parts of a diff that the model focuses on when predicting risk. We aggregate token-level attention into interpretable code units (lines, hunks, and files), and present the top-K units to developers as a lightweight form of guidance during code review. We evaluate our approach using expert-labeled changes that have caused real outages. Results show that the highlighted snippets cover expert-labeled outage-causing change lines 53.85% of the time when highlighting the top-2 hunks, while requiring developers to review 26.28% of the changed lines on average. Because attention is produced during standard model inference, the approach is scalable for large development workflows and can be surfaced in the code review UI with low additional latency.

</details>


### [39] [A Systematic Methodology for Evaluating Failure Independence in LLM-Generated Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02808v1)
*Rodrigo Pato Nogueira,Karthik Pattabiraman,Marco Vieira,João R. Campos*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 该研究系统评估了LLM生成代码的失败独立性，发现同一模型生成的实现高度相似，不同模型虽更独立但仍远未达到完全独立，集成可靠性增益仅为理想情况下的半数以下，表明NVP的独立性假设不成立，但异构模型可部分改善。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: NVP依赖失败独立性假设，但LLM降低了生成多个实现的成本，需要评估其失败是否独立以决定NVP的适用性。

Method: 提出系统方法论，包括结构多样性分析（代码相似性）、行为多样性分析（相同测试失败情况）、N版本可靠性分析（多数投票）和人工故障分析。应用于12个LLM、5种编程语言、3种提示策略共224个编程问题。

Result: 同一模型的结构和行为多样性低；不同模型多样性更高，但失败重叠仍远高于独立性预期；三/五版本集成仅实现独立性下增益的0.43/0.44，同模型集成低于0.3；不同失败模式常共享根因。

Conclusion: LLM生成的代码不满足NVP的失败独立性假设，异构模型有助于部分缓解，但无法完全满足；所提方法论可有效评估未来模型。

中文摘要：N版本编程（NVP）通过执行多个独立实现并组合输出来提高软件可靠性，但其应用受到高成本和失败独立性假设的限制，实证研究已对该假设提出质疑。大型语言模型（LLM）的最新进展降低了生成多个实现的成本，焦点转移到其失败是否独立。我们提出了首个系统性的方法来评估LLM生成代码的失败独立性，并将其应用于12个模型、5种语言和3种提示策略下的224个问题。我们分析了结构多样性和行为多样性（即实现是否在同一测试用例上失败），并通过多数投票下的N版本可靠性分析和对生成代码的人工检查进行补充。结构多样性分析表明，同一模型生成的实现高度相似，而不同模型产生更多不同解决方案。行为多样性呈现相同趋势：不同模型的实现显示出更高的多样性，但在相同测试上失败的概率仍远高于独立性假设下的预期。N版本可靠性分析证实了这一点：三版本和五版本集成仅实现了独立性下可获得可靠性增益的0.43和0.44，当集成来自同一模型时，该值降至0.3以下。人工故障分析显示，甚至不同的失败模式也常共享根本原因。总体而言，这些结果表明LLM生成的解决方案不满足NVP的失败独立性假设，尽管异构模型有助于部分改善。同时，我们的方法论作为系统评估失败独立性的工具也被验证有效。

Original abstract: N-Version Programming (NVP) improves software reliability by executing multiple independent implementations and combining outputs, but its adoption is limited by high cost and the assumption of failure independence, which empirical studies have challenged. Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) reduce the cost of generating multiple implementations, shifting focus to whether their failures are independent. We propose the first systematic methodology to assess failure independence in LLM-generated code and apply it to 224 problems across twelve models, five languages, and three prompting strategies. We analyze both structural and behavioral diversity (i.e., whether implementations fail on the same test cases), complemented by N-version reliability analysis under majority voting and manual inspection of the generated code. Structural diversity analysis shows that implementations from the same model are highly similar, while different models produce more distinct solutions. The same trend appears in behavioral diversity, with implementations from different models showing higher diversity yet still failing on the same tests far more often than expected under independence. N-version reliability analysis reinforces this: three- and five-version ensembles realize only 0.43 and 0.44 of the reliability gain achievable under independence, dropping below 0.3 when ensembles are built from the same model. Manual fault analysis shows that even different failure patterns often share root causes. Overall, these results suggest LLM-generated solutions do not satisfy NVP's failure independence assumption, though heterogeneous models help partially. They also validate our methodology as a tool for systematically evaluating failure independence as models evolve.

</details>

### [40] [Scaling Trends for Lie Detector Oversight in Preference Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01567v1)
*Oskar J. Hollinsworth,Ann-Kathrin Dombrowski,Sam Adam-Day,Adam Gleave,Chris Cundy*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 涉及LLM可扩展监督，与agent可靠性和安全控制相关。

TL;DR: 本文扩展了SOLiD方法至更大模型，发现其在高真阳性率下有效降低未检测欺骗率，并允许移除人工标注，但对分布偏移敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型中的欺骗行为监控成本高，需要可扩展的监督方法。

Method: 将SOLiD方法扩展到更大模型，并在多样化的偏好学习设置中评估。

Result: 未检测欺骗率从1B模型的34%降至405B模型的14%，移除人工标注后无显著欺骗增加；但对分布偏移敏感导致高假阳性率。

Conclusion: SOLiD在大模型上表现出有利扩展性，但需解决分布偏移问题以实际应用。

中文摘要：大语言模型中的欺骗行为监控和预防成本高昂，因此激发了诸如通过测谎仪实现可扩展监督（SOLiD）等方法，该方法利用测谎仪识别出需要由高成本标注员审查的响应。在本文中，我们将SOLiD扩展到更大的模型，并在更多样化且更真实的偏好学习环境中进行评估。我们发现有利的扩展性：在检测器真阳性率为99%的情况下，未检测到的欺骗率从1B参数模型的34%下降到405B参数模型的14%，并且可以在微调阶段完全移除昂贵的人工标注员，而不会导致统计上显著的欺骗增加。然而，SOLiD对检测器训练数据与偏好训练数据之间的分布偏移敏感，这可能会将检测器假阳性率推至不切实际的水平。

Original abstract: Deceptive behavior in LLMs is costly to monitor and prevent, motivating approaches such as Scalable Oversight via Lie Detectors (SOLiD) (Cundy & Gleave, 2025), which uses lie detectors to identify responses for review by high-cost labelers. In this paper, we scale SOLiD to larger models and evaluate it in more diverse and realistic preference-learning settings. We find favorable scaling: undetected deception drops from 34% for 1B-parameter models to 14% for 405B-parameter models at a detector true positive rate of 99%, and expensive human labelers can be removed entirely from the fine-tuning phase without a statistically significant increase in deception. However, SOLiD is sensitive to distribution shift between detector training and preference-training data, which can drive detector false positive rates to impractical levels.

</details>


### [41] [EO-Agents: A Three-Agent LLM Pipeline for Earth Observation Hypothesis Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01584v1)
*Mahyar Ghazanfari,Amin Tabrizian,Armin Mehrabian,Peng Wei*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent LLM流水线用于科学假设生成，通用agent架构。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于NASA地球观测知识图谱的流水线，利用图神经网络和LLM代理生成结构化假设，在1475个数据集上产生160个科学假设，并揭示了单评判者LLM评估的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM假设生成方法依赖非结构化文献和自由文本，缺乏对结构化知识图谱的利用，导致假设的科学性和可重复性受限。

Method: 构建基于NASA地球观测知识图谱的流水线：使用异构图神经网络对历史共现关系学习，对候选数据集配对排序；随后通过三智能体LLM流水线（过滤、生成、评估）产出结构化研究假设。

Result: 应用于1475个NASA数据集，生成160个假设，涵盖多个地球科学领域；模型预测的新配对与文献中真实共现的合理性相近；2×2×2析因实验显示假设排名稳定，但绝对分数高度依赖评判者身份。

Conclusion: 该流水线能有效生成科学上连贯的新数据集组合，但单评判者LLM评估存在不可忽视的偏差，需谨慎使用。

中文摘要：大语言模型最近被探索用于科学假设生成，但大多数先前工作依赖于非结构化文献和自由形式的文本声明。我们提出了一种面向地球观测的流水线，直接将假设生成建立在NASA地球观测知识图谱中。一个基于历史共现关系训练的异构图神经网络对候选数据集配对进行排序，而一个三智能体LLM流水线则过滤、生成和评估结构化研究假设。应用于1,475个NASA数据集，该系统产生了160个假设，涵盖多个地球科学领域，包括生态水文学、冰川学、气溶胶-云相互作用、植被物候学和平流层化学。模型预测的新数据集配对与文献中保留的真实共现配对相比，其合理性几乎相当，表明该流水线能够揭示科学上连贯但尚未探索的组合。一个在GPT-5.2和Claude Sonnet 4.6上的2*2*2析因实验表明，假设排名保持稳定，而绝对分数高度依赖于评判者身份，突显了单评判者LLM评估的局限性。

Original abstract: Large language models have recently been explored for scientific hypothesis generation, but most prior work relies on unstructured literature and free-form textual claims. We present a pipeline for Earth observation that grounds hypothesis generation directly in the NASA Earth Observation Knowledge Graph. A heterogeneous graph neural network trained on historical co-usage relations ranks candidate dataset pairings, and a three-agent LLM pipeline filters, generates, and evaluates structured research hypotheses. Applied to 1,475 NASA datasets, the system produces 160 hypotheses spanning multiple Earth-science domains, including ecohydrology, glaciology, aerosol--cloud interactions, vegetation phenology, and stratospheric chemistry. Model-predicted novel dataset pairings are rated nearly as plausible as held-out real co-usages from the literature, indicating that the pipeline surfaces scientifically coherent yet unexplored combinations. A 2*2*2 factorial experiment across GPT-5.2 and Claude Sonnet 4.6 shows that hypothesis rankings remain stable, while absolute scores depend strongly on judge identity, highlighting limitations of single-judge LLM evaluation.

</details>


### [42] [Hawk: Harnessing Hardware-Aware Knowledge for High-Performance NPU Kernel Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01590v2)
*Junyi Wen,Ruiyan Zhuang,Yongjia Xu,Pengtu Li,Rui Zou,Hongyi Chen,Chingman Wan,Puxu Yang,Wuhui Chen,Yanlin Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Hawk是一个无需训练的NPU内核生成框架，通过硬件感知知识表示和检索，将准确率从49.4%提升到80.0%，执行加速高达2.2倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: NPU高性能内核开发难度大，现有LLM缺乏硬件先验知识，导致生成代码运行时崩溃和性能下降。

Method: 提出Hawk框架，包含三个模块：运行时知识合成（三分可执行知识表示耦合错误上下文与语义）、瓶颈感知知识检索（2D检索范式投影查询到语法和硬件对齐空间）、效果驱动知识蒸馏（LLM仲裁根据执行反馈修剪冗余）。

Result: 在真实NPU工作负载上，生成准确率从49.4%提升至80.0%，执行速度相比最先进基线最高提升2.2倍。

Conclusion: Hawk有效解决了NPU内核生成中的硬件约束问题，显著提升生成质量和执行效率。

中文摘要：为神经处理单元（NPU）开发高性能内核是一个关键的行业瓶颈，要求开发者手动处理隐式的硬件约束和严格的内存层次结构。虽然大语言模型提供了巨大的自动化潜力，但由于缺乏硬件特定的先验知识，它们在NPU上会彻底失败。天真地移植来自类似NPU内核的代码片段可能通过编译器，但会持续触发运行时崩溃和性能下降，因为盲目违反了潜在的硬件约束。为了克服这个问题，我们引入了Hawk，一个无需训练的框架，通过三个核心模块利用硬件感知知识：（1）运行时知识合成模块，采用三分可执行知识表示来将错误上下文与可执行语义固有地耦合；（2）瓶颈感知知识检索模块，实现2D检索范式将查询投影到正交的语法和硬件对齐的语义空间；（3）效果驱动知识蒸馏模块，利用LLM驱动的语义仲裁，通过基于经验执行反馈修剪错误和整合冗余来持续蒸馏知识。在真实NPU工作负载上的广泛评估表明，Hawk将生成准确率从49.4%提升到80.0%，并且相比最先进的基线实现了高达2.2倍的执行加速。

Original abstract: Developing high-performance kernels for Neural Processing Units (NPUs) is a critical industry bottleneck, requiring developers to manually navigate implicit hardware constraints and strict memory hierarchies. While large language models offer immense automation potential, they fail catastrophically on NPUs due to a fundamental lack of hardware-specific priors. Naively transplanting code snippets from similar NPU kernels may pass the compiler, but it consistently triggers runtime crashes and performance degradation by blindly violating underlying hardware constraints. To overcome this, we introduce Hawk, a training-free framework that harnesses hardware-aware knowledge through three core modules: (1) Run-Time Knowledge Synthesis Module, which employs a Triple-Part Executable Knowledge Representation to inherently couple the error context with executable semantics; (2) Bottleneck-Aware Knowledge Retrieval Module, which implements a 2D-Retrieval paradigm to project queries into orthogonal syntactic and hardware-aligned semantic spaces; and (3) Effect-Driven Knowledge Distillation Module, which leverages LLM-driven semantic arbitration to continuously distill the knowledge by pruning errors and consolidating redundancies based on the empirical execution feedback. Extensive evaluations on real-world NPU workloads demonstrate that Hawk elevates generation accuracy from 49.4% to 80.0%, while achieving up to a 2.2x execution speedup over state-of-the-art baselines.

</details>


### [43] [Safe and Adaptive Cloud Healing: Verifying LLM-Generated Recovery Plans with a Neural-Symbolic World Model](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01595v1)
*Junyan Tan,Haoran Lin,Siyuan Guo,Yichen Fang,Xinyue Luo,Tianyu Shen,Zeyu Qiao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM生成恢复计划与神经符号验证，可迁移到agent规划-验证循环。

TL;DR: PASE利用LLM作为规划引擎，结合神经符号世界模型和元提示优化器，实现动态故障自愈，恢复时间减少40%以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖顺序、松散耦合的架构，未能充分利用LLMs的生成和推理能力。

Method: PASE框架包含LLM规划合成引擎（生成结构化恢复计划）、神经符号世界模型（验证计划可行性）、元提示优化器（DRL训练生成最优提示）。

Result: 在真实云故障数据集上，平均系统恢复时间减少超过40%，未知故障场景检测准确性提高。

Conclusion: PASE通过统一LLM推理、模型验证和元学习指导，推进了自主系统管理。

中文摘要：随着基于云的AI系统规模和复杂性不断增加，通过快速故障检测和自适应恢复来确保服务可靠性已成为一项关键挑战。虽然现有方法将大型语言模型（LLMs）用于语义理解，深度强化学习（DRL）用于策略优化，但它们通常依赖于顺序的、松散耦合的架构，未能充分利用LLMs的生成和推理能力。在本文中，我们提出了一种范式转变——PASE，一种规划感知的语义自愈引擎，这是一个新颖的故障自愈框架，将恢复重新构想为神经符号程序合成任务。PASE采用LLM作为核心规划合成引擎，从语义原语库中生成结构化恢复计划。神经符号世界模型通过模拟验证计划可行性，而元提示优化器通过DRL训练，学习生成最优提示以指导LLM的规划过程。这种紧密的推理-规划-验证-自适应循环能够动态生成上下文感知的恢复策略，超越预定义的动作空间。在真实世界云故障注入数据集上的实验表明，PASE显著优于现有方法，将平均系统恢复时间减少超过40%，并在未知故障场景中提高了故障检测准确性。我们的框架通过统一基于LLM的推理与模型辅助验证和元学习指导，推进了自主系统管理。

Original abstract: As the scale and complexity of cloud-based AI systems continue to escalate, ensuring service reliability through rapid fault detection and adaptive recovery has become a critical challenge. While existing approaches integrate Large Language Models (LLMs) for semantic understanding and Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) for policy optimization, they often rely on sequential, loosely coupled architectures that underutilize the generative and reasoning capabilities of LLMs. In this paper, we propose a paradigm shift with PASE, a Planning-Aware Semantic self-healing engine, a novel fault self-healing framework that reconceptualizes recovery as a neuro-symbolic program synthesis task. PASE employs an LLM as a core Plan Synthesis Engine to generate structured recovery plans from a library of semantic primitives. A Neural-Symbolic World Model verifies plan feasibility through simulation, while a Meta-Prompt Optimizer, trained via DRL, learns to generate optimal prompts that guide the LLM's planning process. This tight reason-plan-verify-adapt loop enables dynamic, context-aware recovery strategy generation beyond predefined action spaces. Experiments on a real-world cloud fault injection dataset demonstrate that PASE significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods, reducing average system recovery time by over 40% and improving fault detection accuracy in unknown fault scenarios. Our framework advances autonomous system management by unifying LLM-based reasoning with model-assisted verification and meta-learned guidance.

</details>


### [44] [Autonomous discovery of traffic laws with AI traffic scientists](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01639v1)
*Xingyuan Dai,Yue Liu,Xiaoyan Gong,Qinghai Miao,Junyou Shang,Yutong Wang,Chao Guo,Yonglin Tian,Yizhang Chai,Chao Xiang,Yisheng Lv,Fei-Yue Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自主发现交通规律的agent系统，通用科学发现agent，可迁移。

TL;DR: 本文提出了TrafficSci，一个自主发现交通规律的AI系统，成功重新发现已知规律并识别了新的时间记忆尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交通规律的发现目前依赖专家驱动，而AI在复杂交通领域的应用存在挑战，需要一种自主、可审计的系统来扩展科学发现。

Method: 将规律发现设计为迭代工作流，包括证据范围界定、基于批评者-法官的假设归纳以及观测-干预验证，通过多个案例研究评估。

Result: 自主重新发现三个已知交通规律，并识别出城市驾驶行为中未报道的内在时间记忆尺度，跨城市和数据集具有统计一致性。

Conclusion: TrafficSci提供了一条将AI驱动科学发现从受控环境扩展到复杂城市系统的有效途径。

中文摘要：通用交通规律描述了城市间拥堵、出行和驾驶行为中的重复模式，为交通规划、管理和控制提供了科学依据。然而，它们的发现仍然依赖于专家驱动，需要从异质性观测证据中识别候选规律或通过干预实验进行验证。尽管自主人工智能系统在受控实验室环境中推动了科学发现，但将其扩展到复杂的交通领域仍然是一个挑战。本文介绍了TrafficSci，一个智能体AI系统，它将交通规律的发现形式化为一个迭代的、可审计的工作流程，整合了证据范围界定、批评者-法官假设归纳以及观测-干预验证。在涵盖人口、网络、控制和轨迹尺度的四个案例研究中，TrafficSci自主重新发现了三个已建立的交通规律，并识别出城市驾驶行为中一个未曾报道的内在时间记忆尺度，该尺度在八个城市和两个轨迹数据集上统计一致。TrafficSci提供了一条将AI驱动的科学发现从受控领域扩展到复杂城市系统的途径。

Original abstract: Universal traffic laws describe recurrent patterns in congestion, mobility and driving behavior across cities, providing a scientific basis for transportation planning, management and control. Their discovery, however, remains expert-driven, requiring candidate regularities to be identified from heterogeneous observational evidence or validated through intervention experiments. Although autonomous artificial intelligence (AI) systems have advanced scientific discovery in controlled laboratory settings, extending them to complex transportation domains remains a challenge. Here we present TrafficSci, an agentic AI system that formulates traffic-law discovery as an iterative, auditable workflow integrating evidence scoping, critic-judge hypothesis induction, and observational-interventional validation. Across four case studies spanning population, network, control and trajectory scales, TrafficSci autonomously rediscovers three established traffic laws and identifies an unreported intrinsic temporal memory scale in urban driving behavior, statistically consistent across eight cities and two trajectory datasets. TrafficSci provides a route for extending AI-driven scientific discovery from controlled domains to complex urban systems.

</details>


### [45] [Diverse Evidence, Better Forecasts: Multi-Agent Deliberation Under Information Asymmetry](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01661v1)
*Yuante Li,Yicheng Tao,Kate Zhang,Taozhi Wang,Gefei Gu,Yaxin Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent信息不对称下的 deliberative 框架，通用方法可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 通过设计信息不对称性（将证据分为公共和私有部分）可以显著提升多智能体预测性能，InfoDelphi框架在预测基准上取得12-18%的Brier分数提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多智能体系统忽视信息分配，所有智能体接收相同证据导致从众行为，多智能体效果不佳。

Method: 提出信息不对称性，将证据分为共享公共和私有子集，每个智能体拥有独占知识；实例化为InfoDelphi框架，包含相关性感知证据路由、基于理由的迭代讨论和置信加权聚合。

Result: 在PolyGym基准上，InfoDelphi的Brier分数比最强基线低12-18%，准确率高4-8个百分点；去除信息不对称性后，讨论收益几乎消失。

Conclusion: 输入多样性（通过信息不对称实现）是多智能体推理有效性的关键因素，而非单纯的多智能体讨论。

中文摘要：多智能体系统越来越多地被用于预测未来事件，因为多个LLM之间的讨论被认为可以改善推理和校准。然而，现有方法忽略了一个关键的设计选择：每个智能体接收什么信息。当所有智能体获得相同的证据时，讨论会退化为从众行为而不是真正的信念修正，使得多智能体系统比单个智能体好不了多少。我们识别出这是一个根本性差距，并提出设计信息不对称性来弥补它：通过将证据划分为共享的公共子集和不相交的私有子集，每个智能体拥有只能通过讨论才能到达其他人的独占知识。我们在理论上表明这种分解降低了智能体间的误差相关性，并将其实例化为InfoDelphi，一个结合了相关性感知证据路由、基于理由的迭代讨论和置信加权聚合的框架。在PolyGym（一个包含来自真实世界预测市场的375个二元预测问题的基准）上，InfoDelphi在Brier分数上比最强的单智能体和多智能体基线高出12–18%，在准确率上高出4–8个百分点。更详细的实验证实，去除信息不对称性会消除大部分讨论收益，确立了输入多样性作为有效多智能体推理的关键推动因素。

Original abstract: Multi-agent systems are increasingly used for forecasting future events, as deliberation among multiple LLMs is believed to improve reasoning and calibration. Yet existing approaches overlook a critical design choice: what information each agent receives. When all agents are given identical evidence, deliberation collapses into herding rather than genuine belief revision, leaving multi-agent systems little better than a single agent. We identify this as a fundamental gap and propose designed information asymmetry to close it: by partitioning evidence into shared public and disjoint private subsets, each agent holds exclusive knowledge that can only reach others through deliberation. We theoretically show that this decomposition reduces inter-agent error correlation, and instantiate it in InfoDelphi, a framework combining relevance-aware evidence routing, rationale-based iterative deliberation, and confidence-weighted aggregation. On PolyGym, a benchmark of 375 binary forecasting questions derived from real-world prediction markets, InfoDelphi outperforms the strongest single-agent and multi-agent baselines by 12--18% in Brier score and 4--8 percentage points in accuracy. More detailed experiments confirm that removing information asymmetry eliminates most deliberation gains, establishing diversity of input as the key enabler of effective multi-agent reasoning.

### [46] [Epistemic Goggles: A Pretrained Module that Induces an Epistemic Frame via Gradient Editing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01690v1)
*Joshua Penman*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 梯度编辑干预模型行为，与agent可靠性和安全控制相关。

TL;DR: Goggles是一种通过编辑微调梯度来赋予语言模型认知框架的模块，使得模型能够将训练数据视为虚构，同时保持性能，解决了否定忽视问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模型微调时无法真正忽略虚假注释，导致相信虚构内容（否定忽视），需要一种在不吸收不良行为的情况下训练模型的方法。

Method: 提出Goggles模块，它在微调过程中编辑梯度以施加认知框架，而不是修改数据，且训练一次后可在未见文档上冻结使用。

Result: 模型在虚构检测上从9%提升到91%，同时在GPQA和TruthfulQA上保持或超过基线性能，且框架在持续微调下仍然持久。

Conclusion: 该方法展示了通过在梯度层面施加认知框架，可以在不对齐数据上训练模型而不吸收其不良行为，为安全训练提供了新路径。

中文摘要：对明确标注为虚构的文档进行语言模型微调会导致模型仍然相信文档的核心主张，这种现象被称为“否定忽视”。在我们的评估中，训练在带有此类注释前缀和后缀的文档上的模型正确识别相关主张为虚构的比例仅为约9%。为了解决这一问题，我们引入了Goggles，这是一个学习模块，它干预微调梯度而非数据。在监督微调过程中，Goggles模块编辑LLM LoRA接收的梯度，并将选定的认知框架（模型对其所读内容性质所采取的态度）赋予文档所教授的内容。Goggles实例针对给定的基础模型、框架和LoRA配置训练一次，然后冻结应用于它从未训练过的文档。通过Goggles训练这些相同的文档（现在不携带虚构注释），模型约91%的时间将内容标记为虚构，同时保持能力（GPQA和TruthfulQA达到或超过基线）。相同的架构支持其他框架：可以训练Goggles实例将文档视为“Redwood Research的AI安全评估”的一部分，而不仅仅是虚构。所赋予的框架在持续微调试图推回主张的情况下仍然存在，而先前的干预则会恢复。Goggles提出了一条路径，即在已知不对齐的数据上训练语言模型而不吸收数据所展示的行为。

Original abstract: Finetuning a language model on documents that are explicitly annotated as fictional results in a model that still actually believes the documents' core claims, an effect known as Negation Neglect. In our evaluations, models trained on documents prefixed and suffixed with such annotations correctly identify the relevant claims as fictional only about 9% of the time. To address this, we introduce Goggles, a learned module that intervenes on the finetuning gradient rather than the data. During supervised finetuning, a Goggles module edits the gradients an LLM LoRA receives, imparting a chosen epistemic frame (the stance the model takes toward the nature of what it reads) to whatever the documents teach. A Goggles instance is trained once for a given base model, frame, and LoRA configuration, then applied frozen to documents it was never trained on. Trained through Goggles on those same documents, now carrying no fictional annotation, the model flags the content as fictional roughly 91% of the time, while preserving capability (GPQA and TruthfulQA match or exceed baseline). The same architecture supports other frames: a Goggles instance can be trained to treat documents as "part of an AI safety evaluation by Redwood Research" rather than simply as fiction. The imparted frame persists under continued finetuning that pushes back toward the claim, where prior interventions revert. Goggles suggests a path toward training language models on known-misaligned data without absorbing the behaviors that data demonstrates.

### [47] [COMFYCLAW: Self-Evolving Skill Harnesses for Image Generation Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01709v1)
*Zongxia Li,Dawei Liu,Fuxiao Liu,Yuhang Zhou,Xiyang Wu,Jingxi Chen,Jing Xie,Xiaomin Wu,Lichao Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出技能演化的agent框架，包含记忆、工具反馈与验证，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: COMFYCLAW通过技能进化机制在重复性视觉工作流构建中显著提升智能体性能和可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着工作流重复且领域特定，智能体需要记忆和可复用技能来回忆模式、约束和用户偏好，以提高效率。

Method: 提出COMFYCLAW框架，将工作流构建形式化为类型化图编辑，按阶段组织工具，自动撤销无效编辑，使用区域级VLM验证器将视觉失败转为修复建议，并逐步演化技能库，从先前经验中蒸馏可复用Agent Skills。

Result: 在四个基准分割、三个智能体模型和两个图像骨干网络上，COMFYCLAW在所有六个智能体配置中均取得最佳平均图像生成评估分数，且人工标注显示用户更偏好该框架。

Conclusion: 技能进化是提高智能体在重复性视觉工作流构建中可靠性和性能的有效机制。

中文摘要：智能体越来越多地被用于构建工作流，并协助人类更高效地完成重复性任务。随着这些工作流变得重复且领域特定，智能体记忆和可复用技能变得越来越重要：智能体应能够从之前的运行中回忆工作流模式、执行约束和用户偏好。我们研究基于工作流的图像生成中的这一问题，并引入了COMFYCLAW，一种用于控制ComfyUI工作流的智能体技能进化框架。COMFYCLAW将工作流构建形式化为类型化图编辑，按构建阶段组织暴露工具，自动撤销无效编辑，并使用区域级视觉语言模型（VLM）验证器将视觉失败转化为可操作的修复建议。该框架进一步演化一个逐步公开的技能库，其中来自先前运行的任务轨迹、执行错误和验证器反馈被蒸馏为可复用的智能体技能。在四个基准分割、三个智能体模型和两个图像骨干网络上，COMFYCLAW在所有六个智能体配置中均取得了最佳平均图像生成评估分数，优于没有技能进化的仅验证器基线。人工标注进一步显示，标注者更偏好COMFYCLAW而非没有技能进化的变体。我们的结果表明，技能进化是提高智能体在重复性视觉工作流构建中的可靠性和性能的有效机制。

Original abstract: Agents are increasingly used to construct workflows and assist humans in completing recurring tasks more efficiently. As these workflows become repeated and domain-specific, agent memory and reusable skills become increasingly important: agents should be able to recall workflow patterns, execution constraints, and user preferences from previous runs. We study this problem in workflow-based image generation and introduce COMFYCLAW, an agentic skill evolution harness for controlling ComfyUI workflows. COMFYCLAW formulates workflow construction as typed graph editing, exposes tools organized by construction stage, automatically reverts invalid edits, and uses a region-level vision-language model (VLM) verifier to translate visual failures into actionable repair suggestions. The framework further evolves a progressively disclosed skill library, where trajectories, execution errors, and verifier feedback from previous runs are distilled into reusable Agent Skills. Across four benchmark splits, three agent models, and two image backbones, COMFYCLAW achieves the best average image-generation evaluation score across all six agent configurations, outperforming a verifier-only baseline without skill evolution. Human annotations further show that annotators prefer COMFYCLAW over variants without skill evolution. Our results suggest that skill evolution is an effective mechanism for improving agent reliability and performance in recurring visual workflow construction.

### [48] [Path-level Hindsight Instructions for Semantic Exploration in Vision-Language Navigation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01754v1)
*Sung June Kim,Sangpil Kim,Honglak Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 视觉导航agent中使用后见指令与语义探索，可迁移至agent规划与学习。

TL;DR: Phi-Nav通过后见推理将在线探索轨迹与指令对齐，实现少样本高效训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线策略探索会导致轨迹与指令语义不匹配，缺乏监督信号，而现有方法需要大量专家演示。

Method: 三阶段双监督循环：1) 专家引导在线探索；2) 后见说话者合成路径级指令；3) 第二次模仿学习。

Result: 在R2R-CE和RxR-CE上取得有竞争力的性能，仅需少量专家演示。

Conclusion: Phi-Nav有效解决了在线策略中的语义监督鸿沟，是实现有限数据下训练的有效方案。

中文摘要：在线策略探索是训练鲁棒视觉语言导航智能体的关键组成部分，因为它将策略暴露于更广泛的状态分布中。然而，这种探索不可避免地会导致轨迹偏离专家演示，导致执行的视觉流与原始语言指令之间存在语义不匹配。在这项工作中，我们通过引入Phi-Nav来解决这一挑战，这是一个统一的在线策略框架，利用后见推理将指令与智能体的实际探索轨迹对齐。具体而言，Phi-Nav通过一个三阶段的双监督循环运行：1）智能体执行专家引导的在线策略探索，在从专家动作反馈中学习的同时采样轨迹；2）一个后见说话者基于收集的视觉观察合成一条路径级后见指令；3）智能体进行第二次模仿学习，将合成的轨迹-指令对视为额外的专家演示。通过这个过程，Phi-Nav弥合了在线策略方法中关键的语义监督鸿沟，将无语义标签的运动转化为密集的训练信号。在R2R-CE和RxR-CE基准上的评估表明，Phi-Nav在仅使用当前基线所用专家演示的一小部分的情况下取得了具有竞争力的性能。这些结果强调了视觉语言导航中语义探索的必要性，将Phi-Nav定位为在有限数据下训练具身智能体的有效解决方案。

Original abstract: On-policy exploration is a crucial component for training robust Vision-Language Navigation agents, as it exposes the policy to a broader state distribution. However, such exploration inevitably leads to trajectories that deviate from expert demonstrations, resulting in a semantic mismatch between the executed visual stream and the original language instruction. In this work, we address this challenge by introducing Phi-Nav, a unified on-policy framework that leverages hindsight reasoning to align instructions with the agent's actual exploratory journey. Specifically, Phi-Nav operates through a three-stage dual-supervision cycle: 1) the agent performs oracle-guided on-policy exploration, sampling a trajectory while learning from expert action feedback, 2) a hindsight speaker synthesizes a path-level hindsight instruction grounded in the collected visual observations, and 3) the agent conducts a second imitation pass, treating the synthesized trajectory-instruction pair as an additional expert demonstration. Through this process, Phi-Nav bridges the critical semantic supervision gap inherent in on-policy methods, transforming semantically unlabeled movement into dense training signals. Evaluations on the R2R-CE and RxR-CE benchmarks show that Phi-Nav yields competitive performance while requiring only a fraction of the expert demonstrations used by current baselines. These results underscore the necessity of semantic exploration in VLN, positioning Phi-Nav as an effective solution for training embodied agents with limited data.

</details>


### [49] [Mastermind: Strategy-grounded Learning for Repository-Scale Vulnerability Reproduction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01764v1)
*Mingzhe Du,Luu Anh Tuan,Tianyi Wu,Renyang Liu,Zhijiang Guo,Dong Huang,See-Kiong Ng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 仓库级漏洞复现agent，含策略学习与双循环框架，直接适用于代码优化agent。

TL;DR: 提出Mastermind框架，通过可转移策略学习提升仓库级漏洞复现智能体的性能，在CyberGym上达到84.5%的通过率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体在仓库级漏洞复现中常因选择错误策略而失败，而策略本身比完整轨迹更适合作为学习单元。

Method: 提出双循环框架Mastermind，包含可训练的计划器（通过SFT和基于里程碑的GRPO学习策略）和经验循环（维护局部策略记录），计划器独立于执行器训练。

Result: 在260个训练任务和200个测试任务上，使用GPT-5.5作为冻结执行器达到84.5%通过率，显著优于基线方法，且计划器可转移至其他模型。

Conclusion: 学习高层策略是改进仓库级SE智能体的有效且可转移机制。

中文摘要：仓库级漏洞复现是一项要求很高的软件工程任务：智能体必须检查代码库，推断到达漏洞路径的输入语法，构造概念验证（PoC），并验证崩溃在修补后的构建中消失。最近的LLM智能体在方法正确时通常能够执行这些步骤，但它们仍然因选择错误策略而失败。本文认为，对于此类软件工程智能体，策略而非完整的行动轨迹是正确学习单元：策略足够紧凑以进行优化，足够具体以指导执行，并且足够稳定以存储和跨尝试重用。我们提出了Mastermind，一个双循环框架，将可转移的策略学习与任务特定经验分离。可训练的计划器通过监督微调和基于里程碑的GRPO学习可重用的漏洞复现策略，而经验循环维护任务局部的策略记录以指导后续尝试。计划器独立于执行器进行训练，使得策略学习能够改进多个冻结的执行器，而无需修改其行动生成能力。我们在CyberGym上使用260个训练任务和200个保留评估任务评估Mastermind。使用GPT-5.5作为冻结执行器，Mastermind达到了84.5%的通过率，优于开放书本PoC上下文（60.0%）、Best-of-8采样（63.0%）和迭代改进（77.0%）。相同的计划器还将GPT-5.4 mini和GLM~5.1从45.0%和58.5%分别提升到60.0%和71.0%。这些结果表明，学习高层策略是改进仓库级软件工程智能体的一种有效且可转移的机制。

Original abstract: Repository-level vulnerability reproduction is a demanding software engineering (SE) task: an agent must inspect a codebase, infer the input grammar that reaches a vulnerable path, construct a proof-of-conceptv(PoC), and verify that the crash disappears on the patched build. Recent LLM agents can often execute these steps when the approach is correct, yet they still fail by choosing the wrong strategy. This paper argues that strategy, rather than the full action trajectory, is the right learning unit for such SE agents: it is compact enough to optimize, concrete enough to guide execution, and stable enough to store and reuse across attempts. We present Mastermind, a dual-loop framework that separates transferable strategy learning from task-specific experience. A trainable planner learns reusable vulnerability-reproduction strategies through SFT and milestone-based GRPO, while an experience loop maintains task-local strategy records that guide subsequent attempts. The planner is trained independently of the executor, allowing strategy learning to improve multiple frozen executors without modifying their action-generation capability. We evaluate Mastermind on CyberGym using 260 training tasks and 200 held-out evaluation tasks. With GPT-5.5 as the frozen executor, Mastermind achieves an 84.5% pass rate, outperforming open-book PoC context (60.0%), Best-of-8 sampling (63.0%), and iterative improvement (77.0%). The same planner also improves GPT-5.4 mini and GLM~5.1 from 45.0% and 58.5% to 60.0% and 71.0%. These results demonstrate that learning high-level strategies is an effective and transferable mechanism for improving repository-scale SE agents.

### [50] [SimWorlds: A Multi-Agent System for Dynamic 3D Scene Creation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01766v1)
*Chunjiang Liu,Xiaoyuan Wang,Haoyu Chen,Yizhou Zhao,Ming-Hsuan Yang,László A. Jeni*

TL;DR: 提出了SimWorlds多智能体框架，能从文本生成动态4D场景，并通过4DBuildBench基准验证其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体生成3D场景主要针对静态输出，而动态4D场景（如液体流动、粒子发射等）对视频生成和具身AI有价值但未被充分探索，且动态场景的生成和验证面临更大挑战。

Method: 提出SimWorlds多智能体框架，包含Blender程序化知识、规划器-编码器-审查器工作流程、分层场景协议（由确定性验证器执行）以及运行时状态检查工具，用于生成和验证动态4D场景。同时引入4DBuildBench基准评估视觉保真度和物理一致性。

Result: 实验表明SimWorlds在动态Blender生成任务中优于先前的基线方法。

Conclusion: SimWorlds能够有效生成可编辑的动态4D场景，并通过多智能体协作和验证机制确保物理一致性，为动态场景生成提供了新的解决方案。

中文摘要：LLM智能体越来越多地被用于以程序化方式将自然语言转化为3D场景，但现有系统侧重于静态输出。仅从文本生成动态4D场景（其中液体流动、粒子发射、刚体级联、铰接机构运动）仍然在很大程度上未被探索，尽管它们作为可编辑内容以及视频生成和具身AI的物理基础训练数据具有价值。两个挑战使动态情况与静态文本到场景的工作区分开来：智能体必须在一个连贯的场景中协调空间布局、多个物理求解器、时间序列、相机和照明，并且从渲染视频中验证运动正确性从根本上比判断单张图像更难。我们提出SimWorlds：一个多智能体框架，能从文本生成动态、可编辑的4D场景，具有Blender特有的程序化知识、一个规划器-编码器-审查器工作流程驱动固定的顺序构建阶段、由确定性验证器强制执行的分层场景协议，以及一套运行时状态检查工具，可以捕捉渲染图像无法揭示的机制故障。我们还引入了4DBuildBench，一个用于评估从文本提示生成的程序化动态3D场景的视觉保真度和物理一致性的基准。实验表明，SimWorlds在动态Blender生成基线中表现更优。

Original abstract: LLM agents are increasingly used to translate natural language into 3D scenes in a procedural way, but existing systems focus on static output. Dynamic 4D scenes from text alone, in which liquids flow, particles emit, rigid bodies cascade, and articulated mechanisms move, remain largely unexplored despite their value as editable content and as physics-grounded training data for video generation and embodied AI. Two challenges set the dynamic case apart from static text-to-scene work: an agent must jointly coordinate spatial layout, multiple physics solvers, temporal sequencing, camera, and lighting in a single coherent scene, and verifying motion correctness from rendered video is fundamentally harder than judging a single image. We present SimWorlds: a multi-agent framework that produces dynamic, editable 4D scenes from text, with Blender-specific procedural knowledge, a planner-coder-reviewer workflow driving a fixed ordered sequence of construction stages, a layered scene protocol enforced by a deterministic verifier, and a runtime-state inspection tool suite that catches mechanism failures the rendered image cannot reveal. We also introduce 4DBuildBench, a benchmark for assessing both visual fidelity and physical consistency of the procedural dynamic 3D scenes generated from text prompts. Experiments show that SimWorlds outperforms prior dynamic Blender generation baselines.

</details>


### [51] [Repair the Amplifier, Not the Symptom: Stable World-Model Correction for Agent Rollouts](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01767v2)
*Xinyuan Song,Zekun Cai*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 世界模型修正稳定agent rollout，提出光谱子图修复，可迁移至coding agent失败恢复。

TL;DR: 提出WM-SAR，一种谱子图修复方法，通过选择紧凑子图并仅将该子图提供给LLM进行根因修复，在紧凑令牌预算下实现更强的长时域稳定性和根因恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法修复最明显错误会遗留错误放大路径，而重放全图代价高且不可靠，因此需要选择紧凑子图进行修复以稳定后续轨迹。

Method: 提出WM-SAR，通过估计节点-边放大，贪婪地生长连通的修复区域，并仅将该区域发送给LLM进行根因修复，将修复视为稳定化而非仅归因。

Result: 在合成调用树图、基准启发的代理拓扑和跨模型LLM修复实验中，WM-SAR在紧凑令牌预算下实现了更强的长时域稳定性和根因恢复，与更大修复上下文性能匹配。

Conclusion: WM-SAR通过紧凑子图暴露更清晰的因果结构，将修复视为稳定化，有效提升长时域语言代理的可靠性。

中文摘要：长时域语言代理越来越多地以规划图的形式维护可执行的世界模型，其中工具调用、验证器、内存更新、恢复分支和最终答案通过类型化依赖关系连接。当一次轨迹失败时，修复最明显的错误可能会使底层的错误放大路径保持不变，而重放整个图则代价高昂，且难以被长上下文模型可靠地使用。我们研究世界模型修正：选择一个失败规划图的紧凑子图，其修复能够稳定后续的轨迹。我们首先实例化了一系列强大的工程修正器，包括逐点错误扫描、TopK和窗口选择、局部图扩展、级联修复以及全上下文LLM修复。然后我们提出WM-SAR，一种谱子图修复方法，它估计节点-边放大，通过边际残差-谱缓解贪婪地生长一个连通的修复区域，并仅将该区域发送给LLM进行根因修复。理论上，我们将残差谱半径与轨迹误差和规划遗憾联系起来，将修复视为稳定化而非仅仅归因。在合成调用树图、基准启发的代理拓扑以及跨模型LLM修复实验中，WM-SAR在紧凑的令牌预算下实现了更强的长时域稳定性和根因恢复，与更大的修复上下文相匹配，同时使LLM暴露于更清晰的因果子图。

Original abstract: Long-horizon language agents increasingly maintain executable world models in the form of planning graphs, where tool calls, validators, memory updates, recovery branches, and final answers are connected by typed dependencies. When a rollout fails, repairing the most visible error can leave the underlying error-amplification path intact, while replaying the full graph is expensive and difficult for long-context models to use reliably. We study world-model correction: selecting a compact subgraph of a failed planning graph whose repair stabilizes subsequent rollouts. We first instantiate a strong family of engineering correctors, including pointwise error scans, TopK and window selection, local graph expansion, cascade repair, and full-context LLM repair. We then propose WM-SAR, a spectral subgraph repair method that estimates node-edge amplification, greedily grows a connected repair region by marginal residual-spectral relief, and sends only this region to an LLM for root-cause repair. Theoretically, we connect residual spectral radius to rollout error and planning regret, motivating repair as stabilization rather than attribution alone. Across synthetic calling-tree graphs, benchmark-inspired agent topologies, and cross-model LLM repair experiments, WM-SAR achieves stronger long-horizon stabilization and root-cause recovery under compact token budgets, matching much larger repair contexts while exposing the LLM to a cleaner causal subgraph.

### [52] [Safety Testing LLM Agents at Scale: From Risk Discovery to Evidence-Grounded Verification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01793v2)
*Yunhao Feng,Ruixiao Lin,Ming Wen,Qinqin He,Yanming Guo,Yifan Ding,Yutao Wu,Jialuo Chen,Zhuoer Xu,Xiaohu Du,Jianan Ma,Zixing Chen,Xingjun Ma,Yunhao Chen,Xinhao Deng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM agent安全测试框架，符合条件3，可迁移至agent安全验证

TL;DR: 提出Vera框架，通过自动化三阶段流程实现代理系统的安全测试，在多个框架上发现高攻击成功率，并发布包含1600个用例的基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全测试依赖专家设计和硬编码规则，成本高且难以扩展，无法适应代理系统的快速演变。

Method: 采用三阶段自强化流程：文献驱动风险分类、组合生成安全用例、自适应执行与基于证据的验证。

Result: 在四个代理框架上攻击成功率达93.9%，发布Vera-Bench包含1600个用例、124个风险类别。

Conclusion: 模块化可执行测试基础设施对于大规模代理系统的安全评估是必要的。

中文摘要：大语言模型代理越来越频繁地通过外部工具执行自主操作，导致了复杂且不断演变的安全风险。然而，现有的安全测试针对的是专家设计的安全违规，相应的结果由硬编码规则评估，这使得随着代理的进化，扩展成本高昂。为此，我们提出了Vera，一个端到端的自动化安全测试框架，通过三个阶段的自我强化流程，将软件工程测试原则实例化用于非确定性代理。首先，文献驱动的探索持续发现并结构化新兴风险，形成安全风险、攻击方法和工具执行环境的分类体系。其次，跨分类维度的组合组合产生可执行的安全用例，每个用例指定一个具体的安全目标、一个程序化构建的初始状态，以及一个基于可观察工件的确定性验证谓词。第三，自适应执行在隔离沙箱中运行异构代理，其中控制代理基于运行时观察引导多轮交互，而基于证据的验证器根据环境状态和工具调用证据（而非模型自我报告）判断结果。我们在四个生产级代理框架（OpenClaw、Hermes、Codex、Claude Code）上评估了Vera，揭示了重大的安全弱点，在多渠道攻击下平均攻击成功率达到93.9%；我们还发布了Vera-Bench，包含1600个可执行安全用例，涵盖三个执行环境中的124个风险类别。这些结果表明，模块化、可执行的测试基础设施对于快速演进的代理系统在规模上进行严格且可维护的安全评估至关重要。代码已在https://github.com/Yunhao-Feng/Vera公开。

Original abstract: LLM agents increasingly perform autonomous actions through external tools, leading to complex and evolving safety risks. However, existing safety testing targets expert-designed safety violations, and the corresponding outcomes are evaluated by hard-coded rules, making them costly to extend as agents evolve. To this end, we present Vera, an end-to-end automated safety testing framework that instantiates software engineering testing principles for non-deterministic agents through a three-stage, self-reinforcing pipeline. First, a literature-driven exploration continuously discovers and structures emerging risks into taxonomies of safety risks, attack methods, and tool execution environments. Second, combinatorial composition across taxonomy dimensions produces executable safety cases, each specifying a concrete safety goal, a programmatically constructed initial state, and a deterministic verification predicate grounded in observable artifacts. Third, adaptive execution runs heterogeneous agents in isolated sandboxes where a control agent steers multi-turn interaction based on runtime observations, while evidence-grounded verifiers judge outcomes from environment state and tool-call evidence rather than model self-report. We evaluate Vera on four production agent frameworks (OpenClaw, Hermes, Codex, Claude Code), revealing substantial safety weaknesses, with average attack success rates reaching 93.9\% under multi-channel attacks; we also release Vera-Bench, comprising 1600 executable safety cases spanning 124 risk categories across three execution settings. These results indicate that modular, executable testing infrastructure is essential for rigorous and maintainable safety evaluation of rapidly evolving agentic systems at scale. The code is publicly available at https://github.com/Yunhao-Feng/Vera.

### [53] [CLAP: Closed-Loop Training, Evaluation, and Release Control for Domain Agent Post-training](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01846v1)
*Fangfei Li,Chenyang Zhao,Long Wang,Feng Tian,Zhiyue Zheng,Lv Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 领域agent后训练闭环，含训练、诊断、发布门控，可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: CLAP提出了一个闭环后训练方法，通过数据验证、诊断和回放决定适配器是否适合应用链，实验显示部分改善但存在风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 领域智能体后训练面临数据噪声大、收益不确定、离线与在线不匹配以及适配器发布风险，现有方法缺乏闭环验证。

Method: CLAP方法包括将业务数据转化为结构化SFT样本、决策偏好样本、留出集、风险诊断和发布门控记录，并综合数据验证、目标/证据归一化、奖励/KL诊断、离线门控和应用链回放来评估适配器适用性。

Result: 在五个制造批次上，LoRA-SFT平均总体得分提高0.0098，通过率提高0.0240，证据准确率提高0.0280，幻觉和错误事实减少；但仅3个批次改善，GRPO暴露高KL风险；应用链回放显示RAG必要但增加延迟。

Conclusion: 管理领域智能体后训练应依赖集成的数据-训练-评估-发布循环，而非仅凭训练完成或单次离线分数。

中文摘要：领域智能体常面临业务数据噪声大、后训练收益不确定、离线/应用不匹配以及适配器发布风险。本文提出CLAP（闭环智能体后训练），一种将业务数据转化为结构化SFT样本、决策偏好样本、留出集、风险诊断和发布门控记录的闭环方法。CLAP结合数据验证、目标/证据归一化、奖励/KL诊断、离线门控和应用链回放，以决定适配器是否适合目标应用链。在五个匿名制造场景批次上，QLoRA风格的LoRA-SFT取得了适度的平均收益：总体得分提高0.0098，通过率提高0.0240，证据准确率提高0.0280，幻觉和错误事实减少。然而，5个批次中只有3个改善，部分批次退步，且GRPO暴露了高KL风险。应用链回放进一步表明，RAG对于事实提取是必要的；在相同的3B骨干网络和100个回放案例下，面向应用RAG的LoRA-SFT适配器在价值、核心字段以及答案-证据文档/页面匹配上优于基础模型+RAG，但增加了延迟。这些结果支持通过一个集成的数据-训练-评估-发布循环来管理领域智能体后训练，而不是依赖训练完成或单个离线分数。

Original abstract: Domain agents often face noisy business data, uncertain post-training gains, offline/application mismatch, and adapter-release risk. This paper presents CLAP (Closed-Loop Agent Post-training), a closed-loop method that converts business data into structured SFT samples, decision-preference samples, holdout sets, risk diagnostics, and release-gate records. CLAP combines data validation, target/evidence normalization, reward/KL diagnosis, offline gates, and application-chain replay to decide whether an adapter is suitable for the target application chain. On five anonymized manufacturing-scenario batches, QLoRA-style LoRA-SFT yields modest average gains: overall score increases by 0.0098, pass rate by 0.0240, and evidence accuracy by 0.0280, while hallucination and wrong facts decrease. Yet only 3 of 5 batches improve, some batches regress, and GRPO exposes high KL risks. Application-chain replay further shows that RAG is necessary for factual extraction; under the same 3B backbone and 100 replay cases, an application-RAG-oriented LoRA-SFT adapter improves value, core fields, and answer-evidence doc/page matching over base+RAG, but increases latency. These results support managing domain-agent post-training through an integrated data-training-evaluation-release loop rather than relying on training completion or a single offline score.

</details>


### [54] [Safety Targeted Embedding Exploit via Refinement](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01859v1)
*Joshua Adrian Cahyono*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM安全攻击方法，可迁移至agent安全测试

TL;DR: 针对LLM安全训练主要用英语导致的低资源语言泛化漏洞，提出STEER攻击方法，通过梯度引导翻译关键词语为低资源语言以绕过安全机制，在多个模型上取得高攻击成功率，并迁移到GPT-4o-mini，表明需加强多语言安全对齐和输入检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM安全训练主要基于英语，导致低资源语言和代码切换输入的安全机制泛化不足，模型可能自信地输出有害内容，存在安全漏洞。

Method: 提出STEER攻击，利用梯度引导识别对模型拒绝行为影响最大的词语，通过迭代翻译将这些词语转为低资源语言，从而抑制拒绝响应并保持有害意图，同时迁移到黑盒模型。

Result: 在六个8B开源模型上，STEER在JailbreakBench和AdvBench分别达到93.0%和96.7%攻击成功率，优于随机代码切换和GCG；黑盒迁移至GPT-4o-mini成功率为35.5%。

Conclusion: 仅依赖英语对齐的安全机制无法保证在多语言输入下的泛化，需在训练中增加多语言覆盖，并设计检测分布外输入的机制以提升安全性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）的安全训练主要在英语中进行，导致安全机制在低资源语言和混合语言代码切换中的泛化能力尚不确定。我们表明，这造成了一个认知差距，即模型对于超出其安全训练分布范围的输入会自信地生成有害响应。为了研究这一现象，我们提出了STEER（通过精炼的安全目标嵌入利用），这是一种梯度引导的攻击方法，能够识别对模型拒绝行为贡献最大的词语，并迭代地将它们翻译成低资源语言，以抑制拒绝同时保留有害意图。在六个开源80亿参数模型上，STEER在JailbreakBench上实现了高达93.0%的攻击成功率，在AdvBench上实现了96.7%，优于随机代码切换和贪婪坐标梯度（GCG）。得到的提示词还能迁移到GPT-4o-mini，在无需访问目标模型的情况下实现了35.5%的攻击成功率，这表明潜在的弱点并非特定于单一架构。这些发现表明，主要在英语上对齐的安全机制不能假设能泛化到多语言输入。我们认为，改进多语言安全性需要在对齐期间进行更广泛的覆盖，并引入明确检测并拒绝对分布外输入的机制。

Original abstract: Safety training for large language models (LLMs) is conducted predominantly in English, leaving uncertain how well safety mechanisms generalize to low-resource languages and mixed-language code-switching. We show that this creates an epistemic gap in which models confidently generate harmful responses for inputs that fall outside the distribution of their safety training. To study this phenomenon, we introduce STEER (Safety Targeted Embedding Exploit via Refinement), a gradient-guided attack that identifies words contributing most strongly to the model's refusal behavior and iteratively translates them into low-resource languages to suppress refusal while preserving harmful intent. Across six open-source 8B-parameter models, STEER achieves attack success rates of up to 93.0% on JailbreakBench and 96.7% on AdvBench, outperforming random code-switching and Greedy Coordinate Gradient (GCG). The resulting prompts also transfer to GPT-4o-mini, achieving a 35.5% attack success rate without requiring access to the target model, suggesting that the underlying weakness is not specific to a single architecture. These findings demonstrate that safety mechanisms aligned primarily on English cannot be assumed to generalize across multilingual inputs. We argue that improving multilingual safety requires broader coverage during alignment and mechanisms that explicitly detect and abstain on out-of-distribution inputs.

</details>


### [55] [SkillCoach: Self-Evolving Rubrics for Evaluating and Enhancing Agentic Skill-Use](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01874v1)
*Jiayin Zhu,Kelong Mao,Yudong Guo,Dengbo He,Sulong Xu,Simiu Gu,Yutao Yue*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自进化rubric评估agent技能使用，直接相关agent评价与训练

TL;DR: SkillCoach通过自演化过程规则从四个维度评估和增强LLM代理的技能使用，暴露最终准确性隐藏的失败并提供更强监督。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最终验证器成功太粗糙，无法捕捉技能使用中的细微错误（如选择干扰技能、跳过步骤、错误组合），需要更精细的过程评估和训练信号。

Method: 提出SkillCoach框架，从真实轨迹中推导基于技能的过程规则，沿技能选择、技能遵循、技能组合和技能基础反思四个维度评估，并利用演化规则作为过程监督筛选高质量训练数据。

Result: 演化规则显著提升评估质量，暴露最终准确性无法发现的失败，并提供比仅结果过滤更强的监督信号，从而增强代理技能使用。

Conclusion: SkillCoach通过自演化过程规则有效区分过程质量和偶然成功，为代理技能使用提供更细粒度的评估和训练指导。

中文摘要：技能正成为LLM代理的可重用操作层，编码了标准操作流程、领域规则、工具工作流、脚本和验证程序。在现实的技能库中，重叠的技能使得可靠的技能使用变得困难。最终的验证器成功对于评估和训练都过于粗糙，因为代理可能通过试错选择干扰技能、跳过必要步骤、错误地组合工作流或省略最终检查。我们介绍了SkillCoach，一个用于评估和增强代理技能使用的自演化规则框架。SkillCoach从真实的轨迹中推导出基于技能的过程规则，并沿着四个维度评估轨迹：技能选择、技能遵循、技能组合和技能基础反思。它保持外部验证器作为独立的结果信号，使得过程质量可以与偶然的任务成功区分开来。演化后的规则进一步作为过程监督，用于选择高质量的训练轨迹。实验表明，演化后的规则显著提高了评估质量，暴露了最终准确性隐藏的失败，并为增强代理技能使用提供了比仅基于结果的过滤更强的监督信号。

Original abstract: Skills are becoming a reusable operational layer for LLM agents, encoding SOPs, domain rules, tool workflows, scripts, and validation routines. In realistic skill repositories, overlapping skills make reliable skill-use difficult. Final verifier success is too coarse for both evaluation and training, since an agent may pass through trial and error while selecting distractor skills, skipping required steps, composing workflows incorrectly or omitting final checks. We introduce SkillCoach, a self-evolving rubric framework for evaluating and enhancing agentic skill-use. SkillCoach derives skill-grounded process rubrics from real rollouts and evaluates trajectories along four dimensions: skill selection, skill following, skill composition, and skill-grounded reflection. It keeps the external verifier as a separate outcome signal, allowing process quality to be distinguished from accidental task success. The evolved rubrics further serve as process supervision for selecting high-quality training trajectories. Experiments show that evolved rubrics substantially improve evaluation quality, expose failures hidden by final accuracy, and provide stronger supervision signals than outcome-only filtering for enhancing agentic skill-use.

</details>


### [56] [Spec-AUF: Accept-Until-Fail Training under Train-Inference Misalignment for Masked Block Drafters](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01893v1)
*Tianjian Yang,Meng Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 投机解码训练-推理对齐，可提升agent推理效率

TL;DR: 提出AUF，通过截断交叉熵支持到第一个预测失败位置，改进块草拟器的训练，提升推测性解码效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有块草拟器使用全块交叉熵损失，但推理只接受前缀，导致训练与推理不匹配。

Method: AUF在损失侧仅保留草拟器第一个预测失败之前的交叉熵支持，近似前缀敏感监督，无需额外目标或改变推理。

Result: 在Qwen3-8B上，DFlash草拟器平均发射长度从2.40提高到2.61，六个基准全部提升；迁移到Domino从2.56到2.68；发现衰减基线准确率高但解码差，AUF使位置衰减权重失效。

Conclusion: AUF是一种简单有效的训练修改，显著提升推测性解码的块接受长度，且无需改变推理流程。

中文摘要：推测性解码通过草拟一个目标模型从左到右验证的令牌块，仅提交最长接受前缀，从而加速自回归生成。块（DLM风格）草拟器并行预测整个块，这很快，但使用全块交叉熵进行训练，该损失监督每个位置与真实续写之间的差异——尽管推理会丢弃第一个拒绝后的所有令牌。最近的接受感知目标通过重新加权全块损失来修补这一问题；我们则使用教师强制学习作为动机，说明监督应集中在接受前缀上。仅掩码的块草拟器没有输入侧通道用于真实前缀条件化，因此AUF通过在损失侧仅保留草拟器第一个预测失败之前的交叉熵支持来近似该前缀敏感监督。AUF是对交叉熵支持的单一、解耦更改——没有辅助目标，没有验证器推出，也没有改变推理流程或精确性保证。在Qwen3-8B上固定的草拟器骨干和服务设置下，AUF将DFlash草拟器的平均发射长度τ（在六个基准测试上平均）从2.40提高到2.61，在每个基准上都有增益，并迁移到Domino的双分支头（从2.56到2.68）。两个发现使情况更加清晰：仅衰减基线在共享块掩码上达到更高的令牌准确率，但解码更差；在DFlash上，一旦AUF截断支持，标准的指数位置衰减权重在经验上变得无效。

Original abstract: Speculative decoding accelerates autoregressive generation by drafting a block of tokens that the target model verifies left-to-right, committing only the longest accepted prefix. Block (DLM-style) drafters predict the whole block in parallel, which is fast but trained with a full-block cross-entropy that supervises every position against the gold continuation -- even though inference discards every token after the first rejection. Recent acceptance-aware objectives patch this by reweighting the full-block loss; we instead use teacher-forced learning as a motivation for how supervision should concentrate on the accepted prefix. A mask-only block drafter has no input-side channel for gold-prefix conditioning, so AUF approximates that prefix-sensitive supervision on the loss side by keeping the cross-entropy support only through the drafter's first predicted failure. AUF is a single, detached change to the CE support -- no auxiliary objective, no verifier rollouts, and no change to the inference pipeline or the exactness contract. Within fixed drafter backbones and serving settings on Qwen3-8B, AUF raises the DFlash drafter's average emitted length $τ$, averaged over six benchmarks, from 2.40 to 2.61, with a gain on every benchmark, and transfers to Domino's two-branch head (2.56 to 2.68). Two findings sharpen the picture: the decay-only baseline reaches higher token accuracy on the shared block mask yet decodes worse, and on DFlash, once AUF truncates the support, the standard exponential position-decay weighting becomes empirically inert.

### [57] [Rethinking Complexity Metrics for LLM-Integrated Applications: Beyond Source Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01903v1)
*Zihao Xu,Yuekang Li,Gelei Deng,Yi Liu,Zhenchang Xing*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出HECATE工具，首次评估LLM集成应用中的提示层和代码层复杂性，发现提示层复杂性是独立维度，其结构广度指标优于传统代码指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有复杂性度量仅针对代码层，忽略了LLM集成应用中提示层的行为逻辑，因此需要新的工具和指标来全面评估此类应用的复杂性。

Method: 基于25个复杂性维度生成52个候选指标，通过118个组件的版本历史维护活动作为复杂性代理进行验证，去除代码规模影响后保留10个有效指标，并在20个保留组件上验证泛化性。

Result: 10个有效指标中，7个为新提出的结构广度指标（如LLM调用点、提示模板等），传统指标仅RFC表现出广度特征，Halstead N和V为规模残余；提示层指标在加入代码层协变量后仍显著，最佳指标优于传统指标。

Conclusion: 提示复杂性是一个独立于代码复杂性的维度，结构广度指标能有效预测维护工作量，且具有良好的泛化能力。

中文摘要：集成大语言模型的应用将自然语言提示与程序代码相结合，其运行时行为很大程度上源自提示层而非代码本身。然而，现有的复杂性度量指标仅作用于代码层面，完全忽略了这一行为逻辑。我们提出了HECATE，这是第一个旨在评估此类应用中提示层和代码层复杂性的工具。HECATE的核心是“提示即规约”（Prompt-as-Specification），这是一种受霍尔逻辑启发的形式化方法，将每个提示解释为预期行为的规约。基于已发表分类法中的25个复杂性维度，该工具生成了52个候选指标。我们针对从18个开源代码仓库中收集的118个组件对每个指标进行评估，并以版本历史中的维护活动作为复杂性的经验代理，剔除任何在考虑代码规模后失去显著性的指标。只有十个指标通过了这一检验。其中七个属于我们新引入的指标集；它们并非衡量单纯的规模，而是统计结构上不同的元素，例如大语言模型调用点、内存属性和提示模板——我们将这一属性称为结构广度。在存活的三个传统指标中，RFC表现出类似的广度导向特征，而Halstead N和V仅作为规模的残余效应存活；我们的最佳指标超越了这三个传统指标。关键的是，即使将最强的代码层指标作为协变量加入，提示层指标仍保持显著性，从而确立了提示复杂性作为一个独立维度。最后，对来自六个保留仓库的20个组件进行的验证表明，两个最佳指标持续预测维护工作量，支持了它们在训练集之外的泛化能力。

Original abstract: LLM-integrated applications blend natural language prompts with program code, and much of their runtime behavior originates in the prompt layer rather than in the code itself. Existing complexity metrics, however, operate solely at the code level and therefore overlook this behavioral logic entirely. We present HECATE, the first tool designed to assess complexity in both the prompt and code layers of such applications. Central to HECATE is Prompt-as-Specification, a Hoare-logic-inspired formalism that interprets every prompt as a specification of intended behavior. Grounded in 25 complexity dimensions identified across published taxonomies, the tool generates 52 candidate metrics. We assess each metric against 118 components collected from 18 open-source repositories, relying on maintenance activity derived from version history as an empirical proxy for complexity, and discard any metric that loses significance once code size is accounted for. Only ten metrics withstand this test. Seven belong to our newly introduced set; rather than measuring sheer volume, each tallies structurally distinct elements, such as LLM call sites, memory attributes, and prompt templates, an attribute we call structural breadth. Of the three surviving conventional metrics, RFC exhibits a similar breadth-oriented character, while Halstead N and V survive only as a residual effect of size; our top-performing metrics exceed all three. Crucially, the prompt-layer metrics retain significance even when the strongest code-level metric is added as a covariate, establishing prompt complexity as a dimension in its own right. A final validation on 20 components spanning six held-out repositories shows that the two best-performing metrics continue to predict maintenance effort, supporting their generalizability beyond the training set.

</details>


### [58] [ContextSniper: AntTrail's Token-Efficient Code Memory for Repository-Level Program Repair](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01916v3)
*Chiwang Luk,Matin Mohammad Najafi,Zhifeng Jia,Wei Yang,Xiuchang Li,Jinwei Zhu,Yang Ren,Lei Chen,Gao Cong*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 代码仓库修复agent的记忆选择模块，直接降低token成本，与代码优化agent高度相关。

TL;DR: ContextSniper通过三级抽象索引、混合排序和意图感知上下文门，在仓库级程序修复中减少51.5%令牌和36.4%成本，而不影响修复质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
